Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 50 of 200
Question ID: 613176
- **A previously unknown risk surfaces on a project and creates an issue that is estimated to cost**
$50,000. The project manager submits a change request to adjust the cost baseline and uses
contingency reserves to address the cost.
What did the project manager do wrong?
Top of Form
- **A Did not account for all possible risks during project planning**
- **B Did not include the schedule baseline in the change request**
- **C Nothing has been done wrong. The project manager acted properly.**
- **D Used contingency reserves instead of management reserves**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Management reserves are included in the project budget to address unknown risks.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

According to the scenario, the project manager is performing the Monitor Risks process. The risk
in this scenario is stated to be an unknown risk, and the project manager is using contingency
funds, rather than management reserves, to address the risk. Contingency reserves are included in
the cost baseline to address specific identified risks. Management reserves are included in the
project budget to address unknown risks. Using contingency reserves for unknown risks

---

adversely affects the project’s cost baseline. Management reserves are not included in the cost
baseline; therefore, a change request is required to transfer funds from the management reserves
into the cost baseline. Hence, of the choices provided, using contingency reserves instead of
management reserves is what the project manager did wrong.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Did not account for all possible risks during project planning**
Incorrect. Even the most thorough risk identification cannot account for all possible project
risks, and some risks may remain unknown until they are realized. Management reserves
may be included in the project budget specifically to account for these unknown risks.
- **B Did not include the schedule baseline in the change request**
Incorrect. While the schedule baseline may be affected, there is not enough information in
the scenario to make this determination. It is possible that the change request can be
accommodated without the need to modify the schedule baseline.
- **C Nothing has been done wrong. The project manager acted properly.**
Incorrect. Known risks are covered by contingency reserves. Unknown risks are covered by
management reserves. Requesting contingency reserves for unknown risks is what the
project manager did wrong.
- **D Used contingency reserves instead of management reserves**
Correct. Funding for unknown risks comes from the management reserves and not the
contingency reserves. Management reserves are not included in the cost baseline; therefore,
an approved change request is required to transfer funds from the management reserves
into the cost baseline.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 457, 252, 254-255
Bottom of Form

Question 51 of 200
Question ID: 651367
Resource costs continue to rise and are expected to increase further.
What can the project team do to control the costs?
Top of Form
- **A Hold the cost baseline steady**
- **B Conduct an alternative analysis**
- **C Request more funds from the customer**
- **D Utilize management reserves**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What other options do you have?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

As resource costs rise over the course of the project, the project team must seek ways to control
the costs to remain within the boundaries established for the project. There are many ways to do
this. Of the four possibilities presented in this question, one technique is logical - to determine
and analyze the alternatives. This technique is often referred to as alternatives analysis and used
as part of the Monitor and Control Project Work process described in the scenario. For example,
the team can consider various options for the resources, such as using different materials, using
fewer materials, using a different supplier, removing the need to use the resource at all, and so

---

on. The best option would need to be determined and discussed by the team as they conduct the
alternative analysis. Based on the results of the analysis, more actions to control the costs should
follow.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Hold the cost baseline steady**
Incorrect. The cost baseline remains throughout the project as a comparison metric. The
baseline cannot change without an approved change request. Holding it steady does not
control the costs on its own.
- **B Conduct an alternative analysis**
Correct. One option for the project team is to explore potential alternatives and analyze the
benefits and consequences. From this technique, wisdom on the situation and actions to
control the costs may emerge.
- **C Request more funds from the customer**
Incorrect. The rising of resource costs is what the project manager has to manage by
proper planning, risk management, management reserves, and many other means.
Requesting more money from a sponsor or customer is a last-ditch effort.
- **D Utilize management reserves**
Incorrect. It is true that management reserves are funds allocated for the unknown risks,
such as the unexpected increase of resource costs (assuming this increase was indeed
unexpected). However, utilizing management reserves would not prevent the costs from the
further increase. In other words, utilizing management reserves does not equate to
controlling the costs.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 111

Question 52 of 200
Question ID: 612554
It has been determined that due to the lack of local resources for the new project the company is
about the undertake, the project team members will have to be hired from all over the world. The
project manager has concerns about communications among the team members.
What is the project manager's best course of action to address these concerns?
Top of Form
- **A Implement an online tool to enable the team members to chat among themselves**
- **B Enroll the project team members in cultural training to raise cultural awareness**
- **C Nothing; the business world has been multicultural for so long that there should be no issues**
- **D Funnel all communications through the project manager to avoid miscommunication**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The project manager should be proactive in addressing risks.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The fact that the project team comes from all around the world suggests that there will likely be
cultural differences among the project team members and stakeholders. Thus, the project
manager is wise to be concerned about how these cultural differences will impact
communications. The project manager's best course of action, in this scenario, is to help the team
develop their cultural awareness by enrolling everyone in cultural training. Cultural awareness is

---

an understanding of the differences between individuals, groups, and organizations and adapting
the communications in the context of these differences. This awareness and any consequent
actions may help minimize misunderstandings and miscommunication that may result from
cultural differences within the project team. Therefore, among the available choices, enrolling
the project team members in cultural training to raise cultural awareness is what the project
manager should do first.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Implement an online tool to enable the team members to chat among themselves**
Incorrect. With this mix of cultures, it could be very easy for people to offend one another
unintentionally. Although having an online chat tool might be useful, cultural training
should take place first to minimize miscommunication and misunderstandings.
- **B Enroll the project team members in cultural training to raise cultural awareness**
Correct. Under the circumstances described in the scenario, where the team members come
from all over the world, it is easy for people to make inadvertent communication mistakes
that may lead to a conflict. The project manager should take proactive action to minimize
the risk of miscommunication and misunderstandings.
- **C Nothing; the business world has been multicultural for so long that there should be no**
issues
Incorrect. Despite the increasing number of multinational organizations, conflict from
cultural differences plague businesses daily. These issues may negatively affect productivity
and even threaten the project objectives. The project manager should not assume that
cultural issues will not pose a problem for the project. The project manager should take
proactive action to minimize this risk.
- **D Funnel all communications through the project manager to avoid miscommunication**
Incorrect. It is unreasonable to funnel all communications through the project manager.
The role of the project manager is to manage communications among the project team and
stakeholders, rather than becoming the sole conduit of communication.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 376, 383

Question 53 of 200
Question ID: 613305
With a building construction project underway, the director of finance has retired from the
performing organization and has now been replaced. The new director of finance has raised
concerns about the validity of the project's business case. You have made an assessment of the
new stakeholder's relative power, interest, and engagement level and updated the stakeholder
register and the project management plan accordingly.
What should you do next?
Top of Form
- **A Terminate the project because of the flawed business case**
- **B Review and update the business case as necessary**
- **C Submit a change request to update the stakeholder engagement plan**
- **D Modify the assumption log**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The project sponsor is generally accountable for the development and maintenance of the
business case.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The question implies that you, as the project manager, are carrying out the Identify Stakeholders
process with the replacement of a key stakeholder. Updates to the stakeholder register and the

---

project management plan that you have already made are among the outputs of this process. The
assumption log is one of the project documents which may also be updated as part of the Identify
Stakeholders process. Much of the information about the relative power, interest, and
engagement of stakeholders is based on assumptions. This information is entered into the
assumption log. Assumptions about the new director of finance can be made based on her
concerns regarding the validity of the business case. Additionally, any constraints associated with
interacting with specific stakeholders are entered into the assumption log as well. The incorrect
answer choices represent actions that are not necessary, or a project manager lacks the authority
to perform. Therefore, of the available options, modifying the assumption log is what you should
do next.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Terminate the project because of the flawed business case**
Incorrect. The new director of finance may have concerns about the project's business case,
but it is premature to terminate the project at this point. The project sponsor is more likely
to make a determination regarding the termination of a project. Additionally, the project
manager does not have the authority to terminate a project.
- **B Review and update the business case as necessary**
Incorrect. The business documents, which include the business case and benefits
management plan, are created as part of pre-project work. The project sponsor is generally
accountable for the development and maintenance of the business case. A project manager
does not have the authority to update the business documents as they are not project
documents.
- **C Submit a change request to update the stakeholder engagement plan**
Incorrect. The stakeholder engagement plan should be updated based on the replacement of
a key stakeholder. However, the question states that the project management plan has
already been updated. The stakeholder engagement plan is a subsidiary of the project
management plan. Thus, the stakeholder engagement plan has already been updated to
reflect the new stakeholder.
- **D Modify the assumption log**
Correct. Much of the information about the relative power, interest, and engagement of
stakeholders is based on assumptions. This information is entered into the assumption log,
making this choice the best answer to the question asked.

**Reference:**


---

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 515

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 7

Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 54 of 200
Question ID: 651404
During your project execution, another project that is part of the program to which your project
also belongs, submitted a request for a specific engineer who possesses a unique knowledge that
your project needs soon.
What is your best action?
Top of Form
- **A Assign the engineer to your project before the other project can**
- **B Discuss the need with the other project manager**
- **C Assign another team member to fulfill the role of the engineer**
- **D Escalate the issue to the program manager**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What do you know about the other project?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The scenario surrounds the Acquire Resources process. Acquire Resources is the process of
obtaining team members, facilities, equipment, materials, supplies, and other resources necessary
to complete project work. This process validates the availability of the resources planned for and
assigns them to the project. In this scenario, the planned and expected resource may not be
available for your project. Opening communication with the other project that has submitted the

---

request can help each project manager understand each other's need and plans for the sought after
resource. Acquiring resources in an organization with scarce resources requires interpersonal
skills of the project manager and others involved. Interpersonal and team skills are among the
tools and techniques that can be used as part of the Acquire Resources process. A project
manager should work with others to find the resolution, compromise, or some other agreement
before resorting to forcing or escalating the issue. Therefore, of the choices provided, discussing
the need with the other project manager is your best course of action under the circumstances
described in the scenario.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Assign the engineer to your project before the other project can**
Incorrect. Stepping in front of other projects in an organization without communicating
your intent or need may cause unneeded conflict and break down of trust and cooperation.
Working with, not against, the other project is a better solution.
- **B Discuss the need with the other project manager**
Correct. Interpersonal skills and communication are important when acquiring project
resources. Opening a dialogue with the other project manager can uncover the needs of
each project and work towards possible solutions.
- **C Assign another team member to fulfill the role of the engineer**
Incorrect. According to the scenario, the engineer possesses a unique knowledge. From the
way the question is worded, it is unlikely that another team member will be able to fulfill
the role of the engineer.
- **D Escalate the issue to the program manager**
Incorrect. The first point of resolution for this resource acquisition need is better handled
between the projects and other relevant stakeholders. Escalating the resource issue to the
program manager is premature at this point.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 332
Bottom of Form

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 7
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 55 of 200
Question ID: 610004
- **A client is considering your company for a research project. Your project sponsor has requested**
you to create the project charter. To complete this task, you need the project's statement of work
(SOW).
What should you do?
Top of Form
- **A Create the SOW yourself based on past projects**
- **B Look for the SOW in your organizational process assets (OPAs)**
- **C Request your client to provide you with the SOW**
- **D Ask the project management office to provide you with the SOW**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Part of a project manager's role is to collaborate with the customer and understand the details of
the project.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The scenario is presented from the seller's perspective. The client is the buyer, and your company
is the seller. Since your company is being considered for the project, therefore, to secure the
contract with the buyer (your client), you would need the project's procurement SOW created in
the Conduct Procurements process of the buyer. Asking the client for the SOW ensures you have

---

the official document prepared by the client that defines the portion of work required to be
completed by the seller, i.e., your organization. Additionally, collaborating with the initiating
company allows you to have a better understanding of the project purpose, objectives, and
expected benefits that will help in crafting the project charter.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Create the SOW yourself based on past projects**
Incorrect. Since the project is commissioned by an outside entity and your company is
considered for the work, you would need the project's procurement SOW from the buyer
which is the client in the scenario described. Each project is unique. Creating the SOW
based on past projects makes no sense.
- **B Look for the SOW in your organizational process assets (OPAs)**
Incorrect. Since this project was initiated from a source outside of your company, your
OPAs would not have the project's procurement SOW. Furthermore, since every project is
unique, your company's OPAs may have project SOWs from past projects, but they would
not have the procurement SOW for this particular project.
- **C Request your client to provide you with the SOW**
Correct. As the project manager, you should request the project's procurement SOW directly
from the buyer (i.e., your client) to ensure you have the agreed upon SOW. Also, requesting
the SOW from your client demonstrates that you are proactive and encourages
collaboration.
- **D Ask the project management office to provide you with the SOW**
Incorrect. The project management office may have a template of a SOW, but not the
specific SOW for your project. Additionally, your organization in this scenario is a seller,
while the SOW should be provided by the buyer (your client in this scenario).

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 477, 462, 77-78

PMP Exam Simulator

Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 56 of 200
Question ID: 613508
Two project team members have completed their training and certification activities as defined in
their employee development plan records, greatly benefiting project productivity. You want to
ensure that the organization is aware of their accomplishments and utilize their new capabilities
in future projects.
What should you do?
Top of Form
- **A Update enterprise environmental factors**
- **B Note the accomplishments of the team members in the risk report**
- **C Revise test and evaluation documents**
- **D Share the accomplishments with the team members' functional manager**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What are employee development plan records considered?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The scenario suggests you are involved in the Develop Team process. Employee development
plan records are considered enterprise environmental factors (EEFs) that are updated as an output
of that process. When individual project team members achieve significant training and
development goals, their employee development plan records should be updated to reflect these

---

achievements. Updating the EEFs would promote the accomplishments of these team members,
so the organization might recognize them after the project is complete. Having the employees'
achievements documented in the EEFs would also allow the organization to leverage the skills
and capabilities of the employees for future projects and activities.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Update enterprise environmental factors**
Correct. Employee development plan records are considered enterprise environmental
factors (EEFs) that are updated as an output of the Develop Team process. When project
team members achieve significant training and development goals, these achievements
should be recorded in the EEFs to ensure that the organization is aware of their
accomplishments and will utilize their new capabilities in future projects.
- **B Note the accomplishments of the team members in the risk report**
Incorrect. The risk report presents information on sources of overall project risk, together
with summary information on identified individual project risks. The project manager may
have to update the risk report to indicate how successful training and certification have
impacted risk on the project. However, the risk report is unlikely to gain a wide audience
for the organization to be made aware of the accomplishments and capabilities of the team
members.
- **C Revise test and evaluation documents**
Incorrect. Test and evaluation documents are used to record product and deliverable
focused test and evaluation material but are not used to record team members individual
training and development accomplishments.
- **D Share the accomplishments with the team members' functional manager**
Incorrect. There is not enough information in the question to determine what type of the
organization is described in the scenario. Even if the team members had a functional
manager, sharing team members' accomplishments with the manager would not ensure that
this information is retained and used by the organization in future projects.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 344

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 7
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 57 of 200
Question ID: 613215
- **A vendor on a project points out to the project manager that the customer does not need two of**
the requirements requested in the procurement documentation.
What should the project manager do first?
Top of Form
- **A Ignore the vendor's comment and insist on delivering the requirements as specified**
- **B Contact the customer and ask them to validate the requirements**
- **C Submit a change request to remove the requirements from the scope baseline**
- **D Review the requirements traceability matrix to determine the need**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Who requested that these requirements be included in the project?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The project manager, or someone on the project team, needs to find out why the requirements
were specified for inclusion in the project. The requirements traceability matrix should be
reviewed to determine from where the requirement came. A requirements traceability matrix is a
grid that links product requirements from their origin to the deliverables that satisfy them. If the
team cannot trace the requirements back to the source, then they should talk to the customer to

---

get the customer’s opinion. If the requirements are not required, then an approved change request
is required to remove them from the vendor's scope of work.
Keep in mind that although the customer may be the most important source of requirements, they
are not always the sole source; hence the need to review the requirements traceability matrix.
The requirements could have come from any stakeholder, for example, the legal department who
might recommend product warning labels to be included as requirements to mitigate liability. In
any case, the project manager should first understand the source of the requirements before
taking any action. Therefore, of the available choices, the project manager should first review the
requirements traceability matrix to determine the need for the requirements.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Ignore the vendor's comment and insist on delivering the requirements as specified**
Incorrect. The vendor may have a legitimate concern that should be investigated further.
Adding the requirements that may not be required would be adding excessive and
unnecessary cost to the project.
- **B Contact the customer and ask them to validate the requirements**
Incorrect. The project manager may eventually ask the customer to validate the
requirements, but first, the requirements traceability matrix must be reviewed to determine
how and why the requirements were included.
- **C Submit a change request to remove the requirements from the scope baseline**
Incorrect. That is true; an approved change request will be required if the scope baseline
needs to be updated. However, the project manager should first investigate the claim to
determine whether or not the requirements are needed.
- **D Review the requirements traceability matrix to determine the need**
Correct. The project manager should find the source of the requirements to validate the
vendor's findings and take follow-on steps as needed.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 491
Bottom of Form

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 7

Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 58 of 200
Question ID: 612654
Your risk report shows that project risk exposure overall has grown close to a negative threshold.
Before the next regular meeting, you ask risk owners to present any risks and opportunities that
may affect short-term activities. In the meeting, it becomes clear that risk owners from less
engaged departments did not implement some of the previously approved responses.
What should you do now to reduce risk exposure?
Top of Form
- **A Submit a change request to exploit an opportunity that potentially makes up for the undone risk**
responses
- **B Privately confront the risk owners with the issue and collaborate to remove any impediments to**
the risk responses
- **C Reassign the risk ownership to team members who are in departments that are more engaged in**
the project
- **D Escalate the issue by calling a meeting with the risk owners and their managers to discuss**
disciplinary measures
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Ideally, the risk owners would have been included when planning the risk responses. Why would
they fail to follow through? This may be a question on risk exposure, but it also requires
leadership to manage resources.
Correct Answer: B

---


**Explanation:**

Your project charter granted you a certain level of authority as the project manager, and you are
expected to exercise your influence, leadership and management skills. Interpersonal and team
skills are among the tools and techniques that project managers can use as part of the Implement
Risk Responses process. A private confrontation avoids embarrassing individuals unnecessarily.
You can take the time to understand what is holding the risk owner from implementing the risk
responses they agreed to do. Working together may lead to a more expert or timely approach to
eliminate obstacles and reduce risk exposure.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Submit a change request to exploit an opportunity that potentially makes up for the**
undone risk responses
Incorrect. Exploiting an opportunity may appear to balance out the risk responses that have
not been implemented. However, this action does little to address the issue of risk
ownership and disengaged stakeholders in other departments, nor does it reduce risk
exposure.
- **B Privately confront the risk owners with the issue and collaborate to remove any**
impediments to the risk responses
Correct. A private confrontation is a direct approach to conflict resolution: it avoids
embarrassing individuals unnecessarily. You can take the time to understand what is
holding the risk owner from implementing the risk responses they agreed to do.
- **C Reassign the risk ownership to team members who are in departments that are more**
engaged in the project
Incorrect. Piling more responsibility onto the workloads of familiar team members may
expedite the risk responses but may put other targets at risk. This approach does nothing to
address the issue of risk ownership and disengaged stakeholders in other departments nor
does it reduce risk exposure.
- **D Escalate the issue by calling a meeting with the risk owners and their managers to discuss**
disciplinary measures
Incorrect. Without first trying to work with the risk owner, whining to an already
disengaged department manager can lead to further disengagement. This approach may
also hurt your reputation as a project manager.

**Reference:**


---

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 450-451, 350, 63

PMP Exam 7

Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 59 of 200
Question ID: 613353
After assessing team performance, you realize that the team is not communicating well nor
understanding each other's skills and limitations. So, you schedule a weekend team building
session that will require the team members to be off for two days immediately following the
session.
Where do you record this information?
Top of Form
- **A Change request**
- **B Resource management plan**
- **C Resource calendars**
- **D Project schedule**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Where is the best place to record the changes in a team member's schedule?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

According to the scenario, you are carrying out the Develop Team process. Resource calendars
are an output of the process and are used to identify working days and shifts wherein each
resource is available. This includes project team members, who are project resources. And while

---

there are other documents that might be updated with training and development information,
resource calendars are the primary repository for resource schedule updates.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Change request**
Incorrect. Change requests are used to initiate changes to the project's approved plans,
baselines, and documents. They are not used to record resource calendar updates.
- **B Resource management plan**
Incorrect. The resource management plan describes how project resources should be
categorized, allocated, managed and released. The plan does not specify individual
resource schedule information.
- **C Resource calendars**
Correct. Resource calendars are used to identify working days and shifts wherein each
resource is available. Because project team members are resources, updates to their
schedules are entered in the resource calendar.
- **D Project schedule**
Incorrect. The project schedule focuses on activities and their associated dates, durations,
and milestones. Although the project schedule may include links to resource calendars,
their primary focus is on project activities.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 344, 323

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 7
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 60 of 200
Question ID: 612963
The project you have been managing for several years is now moving towards completion. Some
of the project deliverables have been contracted to vendors. You begin to close the project and
want to make sure all activities necessary for project closure are properly completed.
Which of the following activities would you not perform as part of this process?
Top of Form
- **A Reviewing the project exit criteria**
- **B Measuring stakeholders' satisfaction**
- **C Ensuring all costs are charged to the project**
- **D Closing procurements with vendors**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Work that was outsourced during the project is typically settled before project closure.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The question implies you have begun the Close Project or Phase process. Close Project or Phase
is the process of finalizing all activities for the project or phase. The planned work is completed,
the project information is archived, and the resources are reallocated. When closing the project,
you will review the project management plan to ensure all project work is completed and that the
project has met its objectives. The administrative, financial, and legal closure is performed as

---

part of this process. All answer choices except closing procurements with vendors represent
activities performed during project closure. Individual contracts, or procurements, are closed as
part of the Control Procurements process producing an output of closed procurements. Closed
procurements then serve as an input to the Close Project or Phase process. Therefore, since
closing procurements with vendors is not an activity carried out during project closure, of the
choices provided, closing procurements with vendors is the best answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Reviewing the project exit criteria**
Incorrect. Project exit criteria, which are the conditions to be met in order to close the
project or phase, are included in the project charter. Reviewing the project charter for the
exit criteria is an activity you will need to perform. Since the question asks which activity is
'not' performed during project closure, reviewing the project exit criteria is an incorrect
answer.
- **B Measuring stakeholders' satisfaction**
Incorrect. It is beneficial to obtain stakeholders' feedback while the project is ongoing. But
it is essential to measure the stakeholders' satisfaction during project closing. Measuring
stakeholders' satisfaction is part of the Close Project or Phase process. Therefore, this
answer choice can be eliminated.
- **C Ensuring all costs are charged to the project**
Incorrect. As part of the Close Project or Phase process, a financial closure of the project is
performed. The financial closure includes activities such as closing project accounts,
reallocating project facilities, equipment, and other resources, and ensuring all costs are
charged to the project. Ensuring all costs are charged to the project is part of the project
closure, making this choice an incorrect answer.
- **D Closing procurements with vendors**
Correct. Control Procurements is the process of managing procurement relationships,
monitoring contract performance, and closing out contracts. Closing procurements with
vendors take place during the Control Procurements process, not the Close Project or
Phase process, making this choice the best answer to the question asked.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 123-125, 499

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 7
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 61 of 200
Question ID: 651388
- **A company has been awarded a software development project which requires the development**
team to work at the client's office. The client has assigned each developer a cubicle from which
to perform their work. During a daily standup meeting, a developer states that the team members
are too isolated and colocating the team in a war room would increase productivity and quality.
What should the project manager do first?
Top of Form
- **A Explain to the team that colocation would impede productivity due to the inevitable distractions**
- **B Explain to the team that a war room was not specified in the contract**
- **C Negotiate with the client to make a war room available to the team**
- **D Capture a description of the developer's concern in the issue log**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

How are problems encountered during a project tracked and monitored?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The question describes a situation where a project team member has raised a concern which is
affecting productivity and quality. The proposed solution is to make a meeting room available to
the project team to be used as a war room. The request for a meeting room seems reasonable and
would likely enhance the developers' ability to perform as a team. In addition to the project team,

---

the client also has a vested interest in the success of the project and should be receptive to any
reasonable requests that might improve productivity and quality. Thus, the project manager
should negotiate with the client for access to a meeting room for the team to use as a war room.
However, the question is asking what the project manager should do 'first' in this situation. The
concern raised by the developer is an issue that should first be captured in the issue log where the
issue can be tracked and monitored to ensure a timely resolution. Therefore, of the available
options, capturing a description of the developer's concern in the issue log is the best answer to
the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Explain to the team that colocation would impede productivity due to the inevitable**
distractions
Incorrect. Colocation involves placing many or all of the most active project team members
in the same physical location to enhance their ability to perform as a team. A common
colocation strategy is to use a team meeting room, sometimes referred to as a war room.
Although distractions may be a risk, colocation generally enhances performance.
Additionally, the cubicles have already been allocated to the team and could be used during
times when privacy is beneficial.
- **B Explain to the team that a war room was not specified in the contract**
Incorrect. The question does not specify what resources the client is obligated to provide to
the development team. Even if the contract does not provide for the use of a war room, the
project manager can still discuss the issue with the client and see if they would be willing to
make the accommodation. Additionally, if it is even necessary, contracts can always be
amended by mutual agreement. Increased productivity and quality is of interest to the client
as well as the project team, so there is a high likelihood that the client will be receptive to
the request.
- **C Negotiate with the client to make a war room available to the team**
Incorrect. The project manager should negotiate with the client for access to a conference
room for the team to use as a war room. However, the concern raised by the developer
should first be captured in the issue log where the issue can be tracked and monitored to
the resolution.
- **D Capture a description of the developer's concern in the issue log**
Correct. The project manager should first capture the concern raised by the developer in
the issue log. The issue log is a project document where information about issues is

---

recorded and monitored, which will allow the issue to be tracked and monitored to ensure a
timely resolution.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 340, 351
Bottom of Form

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 7
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 62 of 200
Question ID: 610006
You are managing a software upgrade project for your company. Your project sponsor has a great
deal of authority regarding project decisions, but you recently discovered that he doesn't have
much interest in your project. To complete the project successfully, you need your project
sponsor's continuous support.
What stakeholder management strategy should you use with your project sponsor?
- **A Keep the sponsor satisfied**
- **B Manage the sponsor closely**
- **C Monitor the sponsor's actions**
- **D Keep the sponsor informed**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The power/interest grid is being used in this scenario to define the stakeholder management
strategy.
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

- **A power/interest grid is a classification model used for stakeholder analysis and management**
that groups the stakeholders based on their level of authority (power) and their level of concern
(interest) regarding project outcomes. The classification and recommended management
strategies are as follows:
● Low-power/low-interest: monitor only
● Low-power/high-interest: keep informed

---

● High-power/low-interest: keep satisfied
● High-power/high-interest: manage closely
Based on this scenario, the sponsor can be classified as high-power and low-interest; therefore,
the correct answer is to keep the sponsor satisfied.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Keep the sponsor satisfied**
Correct. A high-power/low-interest stakeholder, such as the project sponsor, should be kept
satisfied. Even though they may not be interested, they yield power. This type of stakeholder
should be dealt with caution. If a high-power/low-interest stakeholder becomes dissatisfied
with the project, they may use their power undesirably which could negatively affect the
project.
- **B Manage the sponsor closely**
Incorrect. High-power/high-interest stakeholders are decision makers and have the most
significant impact on project success. Therefore, their expectations should be closely
managed. The scenario describes a sponsor that has high-power/low-interest rather than
high-power/high-interest making this choice an incorrect answer.
- **C Monitor the sponsor's actions**
Incorrect. It is advisable to check in with low-power/low-interest stakeholders sometimes.
But don't bore them or burden yourself with excess communication. A
low-power/low-interest stakeholder requires minimum effort; however, the scenario
describes the sponsor who has high-power/low-interest. Therefore, monitoring the
sponsor's actions is not the best management strategy in this situation.
- **D Keep the sponsor informed**
Incorrect. Low-power/high-interest stakeholders should be kept adequately informed. The
scenario does not describe the sponsor as low-power/high–interest; therefore, this would
not be the best management strategy regarding your project sponsor.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 512;

---

see also
https://www.projectmanagement.com/wikis/368897/Stakeholder-Analysis--using-the-Power-Inte
rest-Grid
see also https://www.mindtools.com/pages/article/newPPM_07.htm

Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 63 of 200
Question ID: 613021
During the development of the project schedule, your project team identified a few activities that
could be performed in parallel by revisiting some of the dependencies, constraints, resource
requirements, optimization, and reserves. You present the compressed schedule to your sponsor,
who accepted it as the baseline.
What should you do next?
Top of Form
- **A Submit a change request to update the schedule baseline**
- **B Assess the need to aggregate the schedule reserves**
- **C Update the assumption log and the lessons learned register**
- **D Analyze earned value to assess variation in schedule dates**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Look for the outputs of the Develop Schedule process.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The scenario implies the project is still in the Planning Process Group, in the middle of the
Develop Schedule process. There are a few tasks left to do once the adjustments have been made
and the schedule has been baselined. You must also update the project management plan
components and the project documents. Remember, the project team has been revisiting some of

---

the dependencies, constraints, resource requirements, optimization, and reserves. Following such
discussions, two of the project documents to update are the assumption log and the lessons
learned. The assumption can be updated with changes to assumptions in duration, resource
utilization, sequencing, or other information that is revealed as a result of developing the
schedule model. The lessons learned register can be updated with techniques that were efficient
and effective in developing the schedule model.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Submit a change request to update the schedule baseline**
Incorrect. A formal change request is required to modify a schedule that has already been
baselined. In the scenario described, the schedule is still in the development, and the
project is still in planning. No change request is needed to update the components of the
project management plan during project planning.
- **B Assess the need to aggregate the schedule reserves**
Incorrect. Assessing the need for aggregating schedule reserves is a task of schedule
network analysis. In this scenario, the project team has revisited the reserves to achieve the
deadline. Therefore, it is a step that has already been performed.
- **C Update the assumption log and the lessons learned register**
Correct. In addition to producing a baseline project schedule, one of the key outputs of the
Develop Schedule process is to update project documents. The need to keep the assumption
log and lessons learned register up to date is important after having to revisit
dependencies, constraints, resource requirements, optimization, and reserves.
- **D Analyze earned value to assess variation in schedule dates**
Incorrect. Earned value analysis is a tool of the Control Schedule process, while the
scenario describes the Develop Schedule process.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 221

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 7
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 64 of 200
Question ID: 612103
- **A project team is getting ready to start inspections and field testing of the product they are**
building. The team gathers the quality management plan and quality metrics. The project
manager indicates that a few more elements are needed before testing can begin.
What else does the project team need to complete this process?
Top of Form
- **A Quality management software**
- **B Project charter**
- **C Schedule management plan**
- **D Verified deliverables**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which of the answer choices is an input to the Control Quality process?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The team is preparing to do inspections and field testing, implying they are going to carry out the
Control Quality process. The way the question is worded suggests that the answer should be an
input to that process. Of the answer choices given, the only input is quality management
software. Quality management software is considered an enterprise environmental factor which

---

is among the inputs to the Control Quality process. The team can use quality management
software to collect and track errors and variations uncovered during inspections and field testing.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Quality management software**
Correct. Quality management software is considered an enterprise environmental factor
and an input to the Control Quality process. The team could use quality management
software during the inspections and field work to track errors and variations in processes.
- **B Project charter**
Incorrect. The project charter authorizes the project and project manager. According to the
scenario, the team is about to start the Control Quality process. The project charter is not
an input to this process.
- **C Schedule management plan**
Incorrect. The schedule management plan establishes the criteria and the activities for
developing, monitoring, and controlling the schedule. This plan is not an input to the
Control Quality process implied by the scenario.
- **D Verified deliverables**
Incorrect. Verified deliverables are outputs rather than an input to the Control Quality
process described by the question. The goal of this process is to measure, inspect, and
verify deliverables for completeness. The Control Quality process results in verified
deliverables, which later become an input to the Validate Scope process for formalized
acceptance.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 301

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 7
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 65 of 200
Question ID: 651323
With all deliverables accepted, the project is nearing its end. The executives are eager to assign
the project manager to other projects. However, before moving on, the project manager has to
deliver the final product to the customer.
What should the project manager do first?
Top of Form
- **A Release equipment and human resources to other projects**
- **B Confirm the delivery and formal acceptance of the deliverables**
- **C Present a list of quality concerns to the customer**
- **D Move on to the next project to please the executives**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

When is product considered done and accepted?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

Note the wording of the question, "With all deliverables accepted, the project is nearing its end."
This implies that the project has entered the Close Project or Phase process and that the Validate
Scope process has already been completed. During project closure, accepting the deliverables
would be redundant since this has already been done during the Validate Scope process. What is
done during project closure is the 'confirmation' of the acceptance, or, in other words, final

---

acceptance. By obtaining final acceptance, the project manager is essentially 'confirming' the
delivery and formal acceptance of deliverables by the relevant stakeholders. Sometimes, this can
be viewed as ticking a checkbox in the checklist of the activities carried out during project
closure. It is like asking a question, "Have the deliverables been accepted earlier in the project as
part of the Validate Scope process?". If the answer is "Yes", check the box. This would
eventually confirm that the deliverables have already been accepted and that the relevant
stakeholders are aware of this fact and agree that the project can now be closed.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Release equipment and human resources to other projects**
Incorrect. Delivering the final product to the customer is not reliant on reassigning people
and equipment to other projects. Reassignment can be done before, during, or after
delivery. The release of project resources is typically specified in the resource management
plan. Additionally, if there are closing tasks that should be performed by the team members,
reassigning the team members before the project is formally closed is a premature action.
- **B Confirm the delivery and formal acceptance of the deliverables**
Correct. As part of project closure implied by the scenario, the project manager should
formally confirm the delivery and formal acceptance of the deliverables. In other words,
during the Close Project or Phase process, relevant stakeholders should be formally
informed of the acceptance of the deliverables, acceptance that has been already obtained
earlier during the Validate Scope process.
- **C Present a list of quality concerns to the customer**
Incorrect. Supplying a list of quality concerns to the customer is not an action a project
manager should take at this point in the project. If there are any quality concerns, those are
to be addressed by the project team before the final product is even considered for delivery.
- **D Move on to the next project to please the executives**
Incorrect. The delivery of the final product to the customer is conducted prior to the closing
of the project, not after the project is closed and considered complete. Therefore, closing
the project is not what the project manager should do first.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 123; see also Project Management Professional

---

(PMP)® Examination Content Outline, Project Management Institute Inc., June 2015, Domain V,
Task 1

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 7
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 66 of 200
Question ID: 651414
The project manager does not have much power over a few project team members who were
brought in to complete some of the scheduled activities. He knows that a solid display of product
understanding, as well as flattery, goes far with this group.
What are these forms of power known as?
Top of Form
- **A Reward-oriented and politeness**
- **B Charismatic and relational**
- **C Referent and informational**
- **D Expert and ingratiating**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Knowledge and experience is power.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

Project managers must lead as well as manage. While leading and dealing with people, project
managers must tap into various forms of power and skills. It is essential for a project manager to
be cognizant of their relationships and influence with others. There are numerous forms of power
that a project manager may be able to use as needed in a project. Some of these forms of power
may never be accessible for project managers. Some factors are outside of a project manager's

---

control to limit those powers. Awareness of the forms of power enables a project manager to
apply more techniques and leadership styles. Expertise is gained through education and
experience. Others, such as ingratiation, is gained from practice and trial and error.
According to the reference provided, examples of expert power are skill, information possessed,
experience, training, education, certification. An example of ingratiating power is an application
of flattery or other common ground to win favor or cooperation. Therefore, of the choices
provided, a solid display of product understanding, as well as flattery, are forms of power known
as expert and ingratiating.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Reward-oriented and politeness**
Incorrect. Reward-oriented power is the ability to give praise or desired items. However,
politeness is not a form of power.
- **B Charismatic and relational**
Incorrect. Charismatic power is displayed by a project manager's charm and likable
personality. Relational power is the ability to build connections and networks. None of
those are described in the scenario.
- **C Referent and informational**
Incorrect. Referent power is based on references and the admiration others have for the
project manager. Informational power is based on the control of data and its distribution.
The scenario does not present those forms of power.
- **D Expert and ingratiating**
Correct. Expert power is earned by the knowledge and skills gained. Ingratiating power is
the application of flattery or other common means to win favor. This choice most accurately
addresses the scenario, making expert and ingratiating the best answer to the question
asked.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 63, 341

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 7
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 67 of 200
Question ID: 612137
After taking over a project that is in the middle of execution, you are looking for information
about the quality management issues that have been escalated by the team and any corrective
actions that have been recommended and/or implemented.
What is your best course of action?
Top of Form
- **A Look at the issue log**
- **B Check the quality management plan**
- **C Review the quality reports**
- **D Talk to the previous project manager**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

This document is an output of the Manage Quality process and presents information either
graphically, numerically, or qualitatively.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

According to the scenario, you are looking for information about the quality management issues
that have been escalated by the team and any corrective actions that have been recommended
and/or implemented. This is the description of a quality report. Quality reports are an output of

---

the Manage Quality process and include information that can be used by other processes and
departments to take corrective actions in order to achieve the project quality objectives.
Looking at the issue log is a plausible answer choice. Questions like this, where there are two
plausible correct answers, are tough but they might appear on the exam. Issue logs record and
track 'all' issues that arise in the course of managing a project, whereas the information presented
in quality reports is specific to quality management including the quality management issues
escalated by the team which is exactly what the question asks. Although an issue log could have
been used to record those issues, it would also contain non-quality management related
information, which is irrelevant to you in this scenario. Quality reports would provide exactly the
information you are looking for, and most likely in greater detail, making quality reports the best
answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Look at the issue log**
Incorrect. The issue log is a project document that captures any problem, gap,
inconsistency, or conflict that arises in the course of managing the project. Although the
issue log could be a plausible option, another answer choice more accurately addresses the
question asked.
- **B Check the quality management plan**
Incorrect. The quality management plan describes how applicable quality policies,
procedures, and guidelines will be implemented to achieve the project’s quality objectives.
The quality management plan, however, does not include any information about quality
management issues that have been raised or the corrective actions recommended or taken
during project execution.
- **C Review the quality reports**
Correct. A quality report is a project document that contains information about quality
management issues escalated by the team as well as any corrective actions that have been
recommended and/or implemented. Since this is a very accurate description of what you are
looking for in the scenario described, reviewing the quality reports is what you should do in
this situation.
- **D Talk to the previous project manager**
Incorrect. While talking to the previous project manager may provide you with some
information you are looking for, it is unlikely that the previous project manager would

---

remember the details of every single issue. It is not even clear from the scenario if this
individual is still around.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 296
Bottom of Form

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 7
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 68 of 200
Question ID: 651412
The project is struggling. The project team looks to you for leadership.
What should you do?
Top of Form
- **A Work with the executives to reduce stress from the team**
- **B Offer help in analyzing and resolving technical issues**
- **C Provide guidance, motivation, and direction to the team**
- **D Apply the strategic and business industry expertise**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Is there any difference between managing and leading?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

Most place the skills and expertise of project managers into the category of technical project
management. This is the skill set representing those skills of effectively applying the project
management knowledge and competencies to achieve project objectives. Although, PMI has
determined from studies that there are two equally important skills that a project manager should
have in balance: strategic and business skills, and leadership skills. Project managers can
demonstrate leadership skills in a variety of ways, especially when dealing with people and

---

teams. At its core, leadership skills manifest themselves in a project manager's ability to guide,
direct, motivate, and build project teams to meet their potentials and the goals of the project.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Work with the executives to reduce stress from the team**
Incorrect. Reducing stress from the team is part of the everyday role and expectation of a
project manager as a servant leader regardless of whether the project is struggling or not.
Leadership requires more than just working with the executives to ease the stress from the
team.
- **B Offer help in analyzing and resolving technical issues**
Incorrect. While technical skills and knowledge are important to project management,
typically, a project manager would not analyze and resolve technical issues. The project
manager's time is better spent guiding, motivating, and supporting the team. Additionally,
technical skills are not leadership skills but represent the abilities to comprehend the
project work and perform project management duties.
- **C Provide guidance, motivation, and direction to the team**
Correct. Leadership skills of project managers can be demonstrated in many ways.
Guiding, motivating, and directing the project team are the quintessential leadership skills
that all project managers should possess at some level.
- **D Apply the strategic and business industry expertise**
Incorrect. Strategic and business management skills represent an arm of the PMI Talent
Triangle. Understanding the project's place in the organization, business, and beyond are
equally important to leadership, but are not in themselves leadership traits.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 60-62, 341

Question 69 of 200
Question ID: 613634
Your project team has just finished creating the activities list and is now in the process of
identifying and documenting relationships among the project activities. While meeting with your
project team, you notice that a series of activities can be done in parallel but must finish in a
specific sequence. Your team is debating which type of activity sequencing method to use.
What would you tell them?
Top of Form
- **A Activities diagramming method**
- **B Precedence diagramming method**
- **C Project schedule network diagram**
- **D Critical path method**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which activity sequencing method has activities represented by nodes and graphically linked by
one or more logical relationships to show the sequence in which activities are to be performed?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

Based on the scenario described, the project team is performing the Sequence Activities process.
The precedence diagramming method (PDM) is the most appropriate technique for the team to
use in this scenario. PDM is used for constructing a schedule model to show the sequence in

---

which activities are to be performed. PDM can be used to represent four types of dependences or
logical relationships graphically, which, in this case, would be a finish-to-finish relationship
between activities.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Activities diagramming method**
Incorrect. 'Activities diagramming method' is a made-up term.
- **B Precedence diagramming method**
Correct. The precedence diagramming method (PDM) is a technique used for constructing
a schedule model to show the sequence in which activities are to be performed. PDM can
be used to represent four types of dependences or logical relationships graphically. As a
hint, one of these types of dependencies, a finish-to-finish relationship between activities,
was mentioned in the question.
- **C Project schedule network diagram**
Incorrect. The question asks which activity sequencing method to use. The precedence
diagramming method is the technique used for constructing a schedule model to show the
sequence in which activities are to be performed. The project schedule network diagram is
the output of the Sequence Activities process, not a method.
- **D Critical path method**
Incorrect. The critical path method is used to estimate the minimum project duration and
determine the amount of schedule flexibility on the logical network paths within the
schedule model. The critical path method is used during the Develop Schedule process, not
the Sequence Activities process described in the question. Also, the question asks which
activity sequencing method should be used by the team. While the critical path method can
be applied to the project schedule network diagram created by the PDM, the critical path
method on its own is not a sequencing method.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 189-190, 194, 210

Question 70 of 200
Question ID: 651373
- **A request for proposal (RFP) has been sent out to prospective sellers. The sellers' responses**
came back with a much higher cost than expected. However, per company policy, if the
responses meet the specifications and the quality requirements, which the responses do, the
requested service must be selected from one of these sellers.
What is the best course of action for the project manager?
Top of Form
- **A Increase the quality standards**
- **B Update the cost baseline**
- **C Conduct a procurement audit**
- **D Resend the RFP**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

How might the information received from the sellers change the project management plan?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

Cost estimates are based on what is known or understood in the project at the time the estimates
are developed. Based on these estimates, the cost baseline is created. The scenario implies the
project is in the Conduct Procurements process, which is part of the Executing Process Group.
Therefore, the cost baseline must have been already approved before project execution begun.

---

Updates to the cost baseline are among the outputs of the Conduct Procurements process. The
scenario states that per the company policy if the response meets the specifications and the
quality requirements, the requested service must be selected from one of these sellers. Therefore,
the project must select a seller and adjust the cost baseline accordingly.
Breaking the policy or changing the specifications is not good practice, to say the least.
Resending the same RFP to prospective sellers is only acceptable if errors or some other factor
impacting all parties were discovered in the initial requests, which is not the case described in the
scenario. An approved change request will be required to modify the cost baseline. However, this
option is not provided. Therefore, of the choices provided, adjusting the cost baseline is the best
answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Increase the quality standards**
Incorrect. Quality standards are established prior to the RFP being sent to potential sellers
so that the sellers can provide estimates based on the specifications and the required
quality level. Altering the quality expectations after the RFP has been sent and responded
is unfair without proper procedures and communication.
- **B Update the cost baseline**
Correct. The cost baseline would be based on the expectations of the RFP. As the sellers
responded, the baseline should be updated based on the new information. An approved
change request will be required to modify the cost baseline.
- **C Conduct a procurement audit**
Incorrect. A procurement audit is a structured review of contracts and contracting
processes for completeness, accuracy, and effectiveness. The audit will typically take place
after the vendor delivered on the contract, while according to the scenario, the project has
just received responses from the sellers implying no contract has been signed.
- **D Resend the RFP**
Incorrect. The RFP was sent out, and the sellers responded. Breaking the policy in attempts
to gain a more expected return by sending out the same RFB breaks trust and working
relations with suppliers.

**Reference:**


---

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 490
Bottom of Form

Question 71 of 200
Question ID: 613673
- **A university is planning a project to develop a course registration application. To reduce the cost**
of the project, the sponsor has suggested that students develop the application as a learning
exercise. The cost of the project will be minimal, but the project manager is still required to
create a budget. The project manager has the approval to allocate $7,500 for the project including
contingency and management reserves.
What does the $7,500 represent for the project?
Top of Form
- **A Cost variance (CV)**
- **B Cost management plan**
- **C Cost baseline**
- **D Project funding requirements**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which output of the Determine Budget process includes management reserves in the cost total?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The question implies that the Determine Budget process is being performed. Outputs of the
Determine Budget process include the cost baseline and project funding requirements. The
project funding requirements are those funds which are included in the cost baseline plus

---

management reserves. Since the $7,500 referenced in the question includes management
reserves, the correct answer choice for the question is the project funding requirements.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Cost variance (CV)**
Incorrect. The cost variance is expressed as the difference between the earned value and
the actual cost. Since the project is still in the planning stage as stated in the question, the
project has yet to create any earned value with which to calculate a cost variance.
- **B Cost management plan**
Incorrect. The cost management plan is the component of the project management plan that
describes how costs will be planned, structured, and controlled. The cost management plan
does not specify a budget for the project.
- **C Cost baseline**
Incorrect. The cost baseline is the approved version of the time-phased project budget,
excluding any management reserves. The question indicates that the $7,500 allocated for
the project includes management reserves, which means that the cost baseline can be
eliminated as a correct answer choice.
- **D Project funding requirements**
Correct. The project funding requirements are those funds which are included in the cost
baseline plus management reserves. Since the $7,500 referenced in the question includes
management reserves, the correct answer choice is project funding requirements.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 256

Question 72 of 200
Question ID: 651370
The project iteration's costs are below estimates and work is being completed well ahead of
schedule. The resource costs and the scope are being measured in story points.
How should the burndown chart look?
Top of Form
- **A The remaining work line is above the ideal burndown rate**
- **B The remaining work line is below the ideal burndown rate**
- **C The earned value line is below the planned value line**
- **D Cannot be determined from the information provided**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What does it look like to burn down a pile of work?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

An iteration burndown chart is an example of a data analysis technique that can be used as part
of the Control Schedule process described in the scenario. To assist the project team monitor and
control the costs and schedule of an iteration, a burndown chart displays the planned work to be
completed and the associated costs or resources allocated to work. Typically, the burndown chart
begins with the sum value of the work on the left then trends down to the end point of the
iteration. All the work is expected to be done at the end of the iteration. Hence, the endpoint is to

---

be at zero for work and costs remaining. The ideal burndown rate line is that straight line from
the start of the iteration to the last point in the iteration when all the work is to be done. Work
completed faster than planned has a steeper slope than the ideal line. That line is reaching the
zero work remaining point faster.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A The remaining work line is above the ideal burndown rate**
Incorrect. The remaining work line will be above the ideal burndown rate if the work is
being completed behind schedule. In the scenario, work is being completed well ahead of
schedule implying the remaining work line is below, not above, the ideal burndown rate.
- **B The remaining work line is below the ideal burndown rate**
Correct. At the start of the iteration, the ideal burndown rate of the work and costs are
mapped. The ideal burndown rate typically is a straight line from the total of story points at
the start to zero at the end of the iteration. In this scenario, the project is burning points
faster than expected, resulting in the remaining work line to be below the ideal burndown
rate.
- **C The earned value line is below the planned value line**
Incorrect. The earned value and the planned value lines are typically displayed using a
burnup, not burndown, chart. If a burnup chart were used in this scenario, the earned value
line would be above, not below, the planned value line, meaning the project is earning more
value than planned.
- **D Cannot be determined from the information provided**
Incorrect. When work is being completed well ahead of schedule, an iteration burndown
chart will show the line that represents work completed tracing below the line that
represents the ideal burndown rate. Therefore, saying that the answer to the question asked
cannot be determined from the information provided would be illogical.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 226, 116
Bottom of Form

Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 73 of 200
Question ID: 651384
- **A project manager is in the process of creating the quality management plan for a product**
development project. Currently, the project manager needs to understand and then estimate the
cost of quality for a particular process.
What is the best course of action?
Top of Form
- **A Develop a RACI chart**
- **B Create a fishbone diagram**
- **C Construct a RAM**
- **D Build a SIPOC model**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which tool or technique associated with the Plan Quality Management process may prove useful
in understanding and estimating the cost of quality for a process?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The quality management plan is created as an output of the Plan Quality Management process.
Tools and techniques that may be used in the development of the quality management plan
include flowcharts. A SIPOC (suppliers, inputs, process, outputs, and customers) model is a type
of flowchart that may prove useful in understanding and estimating the cost of quality for a

---

process. The incorrect answer choices represent tools and techniques that may be used in various
project management processes but are not likely to be useful in the development of the quality
management plan. Therefore, of the available choices, the best course of action for the project
manager is to build a SIPOC model.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Develop a RACI chart**
Incorrect. A RACI chart is a common type of responsibility assignment matrix that uses
responsible, accountable, consult, and inform statuses to define the involvement of
stakeholders in project activities. A RACI chart is more likely to be developed during the
Plan Resource Management process, while the question implies that the Plan Quality
Management process is currently underway.
- **B Create a fishbone diagram**
Incorrect. A cause and effect diagram (also known as a fishbone diagram) is a
decomposition technique that helps trace an undesirable effect back to its root cause. A
cause and effect diagram may be used in various processes throughout a project. However,
the question is asking about estimating the cost of quality for a process rather than the
identification of the root cause of a problem.
- **C Construct a RAM**
Incorrect. A responsibility assignment matrix (RAM) is a grid that shows the project
resources assigned to each work package. A RAM is most helpful in the creation of a
resource management plan, whereas the question states that the project manager is
developing the quality management plan.
- **D Build a SIPOC model**
Correct. A SIPOC (suppliers, inputs, process, outputs, and customers) model a type of
flowchart that may prove useful in understanding and estimating the cost of quality for a
process.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 284-285
