Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 98 of 200
Question ID: 651396
The product trade show is approaching. The project team must produce functional prototypes for
the event. The team is also tasked with many other competing project tasks.
What can the project manager do in the next iteration planning?
Top of Form
- **A Remove the other competing tasks from the schedule**
- **B Reprioritize the remaining work in the product backlog**
- **C Crash the project schedule by adding more resources**
- **D Move the prototype work to be on the critical path**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What is the purpose of iteration planning as it pertains to the product backlog?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The scenario implies the project manager is concerned with the Control Schedule process on a
project managed using agile approaches. Such projects leverage the prioritization of the work on
the product backlog to influence and control the project's schedule and iterations. Due to the
iterative nature of agile managed projects, the schedule is controlled in some manner during
iteration planning - which occurs between iterations. In the scenario, the prototype work and the
other project tasks may all worked on concurrently and with equal importance. Reprioritizing the

---

items on the product backlog allows the project manager and the project team to control the work
scheduled for the upcoming iteration. So if the prototype work is of more focus in the near team
schedule, the backlog should be prioritized accordingly.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Remove the other competing tasks from the schedule**
Incorrect. Tasks cannot be removed from the schedule at will. Such decisions should be
made with the relevant stakeholders. It is likely that a change request will be required to
make any changes to the project scope or schedule.
- **B Reprioritize the remaining work in the product backlog**
Correct. Part of controlling the schedule in an agile-based project is to prioritize the items
on the product backlog to better control the iteration schedules. In other words, when an
agile approach is used, the Control Schedule process is concerned with reprioritizing the
remaining work plan (backlog).
- **C Crash the project schedule by adding more resources**
Incorrect. Crashing is a schedule compression technique used to shorten the schedule
duration for the least incremental cost by adding resources. While this technique could be a
plausible option, there is not enough information in the question to determine if crashing is
the right choice in the scenario described. Applying crashing without considering other
alternatives is not the best course of action.
- **D Move the prototype work to be on the critical path**
Incorrect. The critical path is not based on the criticality of the activities based in a scope
sense, but on a time-based condition. The critical path is a collection of dependent
activities that are expected to take the longest amount of time to complete based on
duration estimates.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 224

Question 99 of 200
Question ID: 651364
- **A team member responsible for tracking the costs of a project increases the budget to**
accommodate the unexpected rise in expenditures over the last three weeks.
What should the project manager say to the project team member?
Top of Form
- **A Any increase to the authorized budget can only be approved via the Perform Integrated Change**
Control process.
- **B If the increase in the budget is to cover an unexpected rise in expenditures, the project sponsor**
should be consulted.
- **C Adjustments to the project budget need to occur closer to the point when expenditures go above**
budget.
- **D Any increase in the authorized budget requires the development of an earned value analysis**
report (EVA) first.
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Is there a procedure or process for making changes to budgets?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The scenario implies the Control Costs process is underway. Controlling the costs of the project
requires the project to stay within the bounds of the budget set for the project. At times, the

---

project may need to adjust the authorized budget, but this can only be done upon approval
through the Perform Integrated Change Control process. The request to make budgetary changes
comes as an output from the Control Costs process. The request(s) are evaluated per the Perform
Integrated Change Control process suitable for the project. If accepted, the approved change to
the budget is what the project team monitors and controls the cost of the project against. A
project team member or project manager cannot make such a change to the budget without
following the process.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Any increase to the authorized budget can only be approved via the Perform Integrated**
Change Control process.
Correct. Any changes to the project's budget must be approved by way of the Perform
Integrated Change Control process. Unauthorized adjustments to the project's budget are
not allowed.
- **B If the increase in the budget is to cover an unexpected rise in expenditures, the project**
sponsor should be consulted.
Incorrect. Unexpected expenditures are common in projects. Various tools and techniques,
such as contingency or management reserves, exist to handle those situations. A procedure
to handle such an increase should be defined in the corresponding components of the
project management plan. The procedure may or may not specify the project sponsor as an
individual to approve the increase.
- **C Adjustments to the project budget need to occur closer to the point when expenditures go**
above budget.
Incorrect. Any changes or adjustments to the authorized budget must go thru the Perform
Integrated Change Control process. The timing does not change the process need.
Adjustments to the project budget need to occur once the corresponding change has been
approved which would typically indicate the target implementation date.
- **D Any increase in the authorized budget requires the development of an earned value**
analysis report (EVA) first.
Incorrect. Approved changes to the budget are not determinant on the earned value
analysis (EVA), even though that information is often relied on to make those change
decisions. The EVA report is not a requirement.

**Reference:**


---

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 259

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 7
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 100 of 200
Question ID: 651439
Your project is trending to meet or exceed all of its objectives, but the spend rate is higher than
planned.
Which of the following most accurately describes the project's performance?
Top of Form
- **A The cost performance index (CPI) is less than 1.0**
- **B The schedule performance index (SPI) is greater than 1.0**
- **C The earned value is less than the planned value**
- **D The to-complete performance index (TCPI) is greater than 1.0**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Eliminate the answer choices that indicate the project is trending to miss a baseline.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The question indicates that the project is trending to meet or exceed all of its objectives. This
means that if the current performance is maintained for the remainder of the project, the entire
project scope will be completed on time or sooner and within or under budget. The spend rate
only indicates that project costs have exceeded what was planned at this point in the project. The
spend rate does not indicate if the actual costs have exceeded the value of the work completed. If
the project work is being completed faster than planned, then it is possible to have a higher than

---

expected spend rate with the project still trending to complete within budget. Thus, just because
a project is spending money at a faster rate than planned, does not necessarily mean that the
project's objectives are in jeopardy. All of the incorrect answer choices can be eliminated
because they indicate that the project is trending to miss a project baseline. An SPI of greater
than 1.0 indicates that the project is trending ahead of schedule, and is the only answer choice
that is aligned with the scenario, according to which the project is trending to meet or exceed all
of its objectives.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A The cost performance index (CPI) is less than 1.0**
Incorrect. The formula to calculate the cost performance index (CPI) can be expressed as
CPI = EV / AC, where EV is earned value and AC is actual cost. A CPI of less than 1.0
indicates a cost overrun for completed work, and the project is trending to miss the cost
baseline. However, the question states that the project is trending to meet or exceed all of
its objectives.
- **B The schedule performance index (SPI) is greater than 1.0**
Correct. The formula to calculate the schedule performance index (SPI) can be expressed
as SPI = EV / PV, where EV is earned value and PV is planned value. An SPI of greater
than 1.0 indicates that the project is trending to complete ahead of schedule, i.e. meet or
exceed all of its objectives as stated by the scenario.
- **C The earned value is less than the planned value**
Incorrect. This answer choice describes a negative schedule variance. The schedule
variance (SV) can be expressed as EV - PV, where EV is earned value and PV is planned
value. If the earned value is less than the planned value, then the schedule variance must be
negative. A negative schedule variance indicates that the project is running behind
schedule. However, the question states that the project is trending to meet or exceed all of
its objectives.
- **D The to-complete performance index (TCPI) is greater than 1.0**
Incorrect. The to-complete performance index (TCPI) is a measure of the cost performance
that must be maintained for the remainder of the project to complete as planned. A TCPI of
greater than 1.0 indicates that the work completed has cost more than planned, and the
project is trending to miss the cost baseline. However, according to the scenario, the project
is trending to meet or exceed all of its objectives.

**Reference:**


---

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 259-263
Bottom of Form
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results
Bottom of Form Prev Next

Question 101 of 200
Question ID: 651400
Sharing of project information is of utmost importance to the organization. Project knowledge is
shared on multiple systems, services, and apps. The array of locations is becoming
overwhelming for some of the project team members.
What is the best option for the project manager to manage the project knowledge in this
situation?
Top of Form
- **A Close down some of the systems that the project team notes as burdensome**
- **B Consolidate or streamline sharing processes where possible**
- **C Compromise with the team to allow each to post in the tool they find most productive**
- **D Coordinate a weekly meeting to post all the team's knowledge at once**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Any room for improvement?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The scenario surrounds the Manage Project Knowledge process. Managing the vast array of
project knowledge is challenging, but important. Often, projects and their organizations use a
variety of tools and systems to collect, distribute, and access that knowledge. Juggling the
volume of the knowledge and its flow adds to the challenge. Ensuring the project team members

---

and other stakeholders use the tools well enhances the timeliness and accessibility of project
information. The project manager and others can and should continuously seek out ways to
improve project processes. This includes the managing of project knowledge and the tools. If
there are ways to consolidate, streamline, et cetera, then efforts should be made to do so.
Ignoring or not following processes does not make the process better, it only makes it worse.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Close down some of the systems that the project team notes as burdensome**
Incorrect. The project manager cannot remove organizational tools simply because some
project team members find it burdensome. The project manager can instead work with the
owners of the tools to improve, clarify, or close any inefficient knowledge repository.
- **B Consolidate or streamline sharing processes where possible**
Correct. Assisting the team in managing of project knowledge to be more effective and
efficient is a good use of a project manager's time. Seeking improvements and removing
constraints aids the knowledge sharing thus improving project performance.
- **C Compromise with the team to allow each to post in the tool they find most productive**
Incorrect. Listening to the needs of the team is one of the project manager's duties.
However, compromising and allowing each team member to post knowledge in the tool they
find most productive may result in project knowledge spread across many locations. This
situation may lead the knowledge becoming less accessible and the team less productive.
- **D Coordinate a weekly meeting to post all the team's knowledge at once**
Incorrect. Project knowledge grows and expands frequently during a project. Withholding
sharing of project knowledge to once a week may not be productive. But more so, the issue
is not strictly the timing, but the number of tools and/or their processes.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 98-100

Question 102 of 200
Question ID: 613313
During execution of a hotel construction project, the person responsible for implementing a
particular risk response strategy has left the performing organization, and the project manager
has identified a new stakeholder to assume those responsibilities.
After updating the stakeholder register, what should the project manager do next?
Top of Form
- **A Update the risk management plan**
- **B Revise the risk register**
- **C Notify the PMO of the new stakeholder**
- **D Execute the Perform Qualitative Risk Analysis process**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Where are the names of nominated risk owners captured?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The question suggests that the project manager is performing the Identify Stakeholders process
by updating the stakeholder register to reflect the addition of a new stakeholder. The question
also indicates that the new stakeholder will assume the responsibilities as a risk owner from the
previous stakeholder. The risk owner is the person responsible for monitoring the risks and for
selecting and implementing an appropriate risk response strategy. The name of the nominated

---

risk owner for each identified risk should be captured in the risk register. The incorrect answer
choices are all unnecessary steps in this scenario. Therefore, of the available choices, revising the
risk register is what the project manager should do next.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Update the risk management plan**
Incorrect. The risk management plan may need to be updated in this scenario. However, the
project manager must first seek an approved change request before the risk management
plan, as a component of the project management plan, can be updated.
- **B Revise the risk register**
Correct. The risk owner is the person responsible for monitoring the risks and for selecting
and implementing an appropriate risk response strategy. The name of the nominated risk
owner for each identified risk should be captured in the risk register.
- **C Notify the PMO of the new stakeholder**
Incorrect. There is not enough information in the question to determine if the company
policy and procedures require the project management office (PMO) to be notified of each
newly identified stakeholder. Typically, it is not the case.
- **D Execute the Perform Qualitative Risk Analysis process**
Incorrect. There is nothing in the scenario to suggest that new risks have been identified
warranting the iteration of the Perform Qualitative Risk Analysis process. While new
stakeholders may become a source of new risks, the question is focusing on risk responses
for which this stakeholder will be responsible rather than on new risks associated with the
stakeholder.

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**

Question 103 of 200
Question ID: 613367
You are managing a project to build a 50 story residential building. When the project was in
planning, the truck drivers threatened to strike, which would prevent the timely delivery of
materials and supplies to the worksite. This risk was identified, and a response plan was
developed. Fortunately, the labor dispute was settled, and the physical resources should be
available as originally planned.
With the threat of the strike averted, what should you do next?
Top of Form
- **A Modify the resource breakdown structure**
- **B Update the lessons learned register**
- **C Update the issue log**
- **D Revise the risk register**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Where are outputs of risk management processes are recorded?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The question describes a situation where a risk had been identified that would have affected
resource availability. With the strike averted, the physical resources will be available as
originally planned. The risk register is a repository in which outputs of risk management

---

processes are recorded. The status of each identified risk is typically included in the risk register.
With the risk of a strike averted, the next logical step is to close out the risk in the risk register.
The incorrect answer choices represent actions that will not be necessary since the risk was not
realized. Therefore, of the available choices, revising the risk register is the best response.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Modify the resource breakdown structure**
Incorrect. The resource breakdown structure is a hierarchical representation of resources
by category and type. The question indicates that the strike had been averted and the
physical resources will be available as originally planned. Therefore, there is no reason to
update the resource breakdown structure.
- **B Update the lessons learned register**
Incorrect. The lessons learned register captures knowledge gained throughout the project.
As it pertains to resource management, the lessons learned register can be updated with
techniques that were effective in managing resource logistics, scrap, utilization variances,
and corrective actions that were used to respond to resource variances. Nothing in the
question indicates that any of those have happened.
- **C Update the issue log**
Incorrect. The issue log is a project document where information about issues is recorded
and monitored. If the risk of a strike had been realized, the problem with resource
availability should have been captured in the issue log. However, in this case, the strike was
averted so there is no issue that needs to be recorded in the issue log. Note that the issue
log contains actual issues encountered on the project and not potential issues.
- **D Revise the risk register**
Correct. The risk register is a repository in which outputs of risk management processes are
recorded. With the risk of a strike averted, the next logical step is to close out the risk in the
risk register.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 358

Question 104 of 200
Question ID: 613753
- **A project manager is preparing for a meeting to identify risks associated with the project. As part**
of the preparations, the project manager is looking for a document that captures a comprehensive
list of factors that could either benefit or constrain the project.
Which of the following would help the project manager the most?
Top of Form
- **A Assumption log**
- **B Project charter**
- **C Risk register**
- **D Assumption register**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What project document serves as an input to the Identify Risks process and contains a
comprehensive list of assumptions that have been made on the project?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The question states that the project is in the planning stage and implies that the project manager
is carrying out the Identify Risks process. One input to the Identify Risks process is the
assumption log. An assumption is a factor in a planning process that is considered to be true,
real, or certain, without proof or demonstration. A constraint is a limiting factor that affects the

---

execution of a project, program, portfolio, or process. The assumption log is a project document
used to record all assumptions and constraints throughout the project life cycle. The assumption
log is the best source for a comprehensive list of assumptions that have been made about the
project up to that point.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Assumption log**
Correct. The assumption log is a project document used to record all assumptions and
constraints throughout the project life cycle. The assumption log is the best source for a
comprehensive list of assumptions that have been made about the project up to that point.
- **B Project charter**
Incorrect. The project charter is the document issued by the sponsor that authorizes the
existence of the project. While the project charter does contain high-level information
about the project including overall project risk and high-level assumptions, it does not
contain a ‘comprehensive’ list of assumptions that have been made about the project.
- **C Risk register**
Incorrect. The risk register captures details of identified project risks. The question implies
that the project manager is performing the Identify Risks process. The risk register is an
output of that process and, therefore, is not yet available at the point of time described in
the scenario.
- **D Assumption register**
Incorrect. 'Assumption register' is a fake term made up for this question.

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 412

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 7
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 105 of 200
Question ID: 613209
Per organizational policy, vendors should be selected by an evaluation committee. The project
manager schedules a meeting to discuss the proposals submitted by prospective vendors but,
based on past experience, is concerned that the committee members may have preconceived
opinions about which vendor should be selected based on personal preferences and relationships.
What is the best course of action for the project manager to select a vendor?
Top of Form
- **A Remove vendors' identifying information from their proposals and let the committee evaluate the**
proposals against the source selection criteria
- **B Hold the meeting as scheduled and let the committee evaluate the vendors' proposals against the**
source selection criteria
- **C Escalate the issue to the project sponsor since preconceived opinions of the committee members**
are outside the control of the project manager
- **D Cancel the meeting to avoid bias and select the vendor based on the merits of the proposals and**
the source selection criteria
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

How might personal biases be eliminated from the selection process?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**


---

The project manager should ensure that vendors are selected objectively by establishing a fair
and objective vendor proposal evaluation process. Although using the established source
selection criteria will set objective selection standards, it may be unrealistic for the source
selection criteria to cover every nuance of the submitted proposals. Thus, even with the use of
the source selection criteria, the risk of personal biases influencing the vendor selection process
may still exist. By removing any identifying information from the proposals and using the
established source selection criteria, the project manager can ensure that each proposal is
evaluated objectively and fairly. Therefore, of the available options, the best course of action for
the project manager is to remove vendors' identifying information from their proposals and let
the committee evaluate the proposals against the source selection criteria.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Remove vendors' identifying information from their proposals and let the committee**
evaluate the proposals against the source selection criteria
Correct. The seller proposals should be evaluated objectively based on the merits of the
proposals rather than personal biases. Removing any identifying information from the
proposals would eliminate any influence from personal biases.
- **B Hold the meeting as scheduled and let the committee evaluate the vendors' proposals**
against the source selection criteria
Incorrect. Holding the meeting as scheduled would ignore the fact that some of the
committee members are biased. This situation may result in selecting the vendor that is not
properly vetted against the source selection criteria and therefore is not the best for the
project, thus reducing the chances of project success.
- **C Escalate the issue to the project sponsor since preconceived opinions of the committee**
members are outside the control of the project manager
Incorrect. While it is true that personal preferences of the committee members are likely
outside the control of the project manager, there are proactive steps that can be done by the
project manager before the issue should be escalated to the project sponsor.
- **D Cancel the meeting to avoid bias and select the vendor based on the merits of the**
proposals and the source selection criteria
Incorrect. Although making the decision without the participation of the evaluation
committee would address the issue of personal biases, bypassing the committee would
violate the organizational policy that requires vendors to be selected by an evaluation
committee.

---


**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 486

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 7
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 106 of 200
Question ID: 612940
The project team has spent a great deal of time reviewing a set of significant changes that a
vendor proposed to the specifications of a project deliverable. Everyone eventually agrees that
the changes would improve the deliverable without any net effect on the cost.
What should be done next?
Top of Form
- **A Implement the changes since no additional costs are involved**
- **B Issue a change request to update the procurement management plan**
- **C Issue a change request to update the project management plan**
- **D Deduct the cost of the evaluation process from the vendor's invoice**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The question describes what could be a far-reaching change.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

Since the change seems to be substantial, there are likely many areas of the project that will be
affected. Even if the cost baseline is not impacted, the scope and schedule baselines may need to
be revised. Additionally, other elements of the project management plan may be affected
including the procurement management plan, requirements management plan, quality
management plan, risk management plan, and perhaps others. Therefore, a change request needs

---

to be issued to review the total impact of the proposed change. Since the project management
plan, including baselines, is considered a configuration element, an approved change request will
be required to implement the proposed changes. Therefore, of the available options, issuing a
change request to update the project management plan is what should be done next.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Implement the changes since no additional costs are involved**
Incorrect. Even if project costs are not affected, the proposed changes may have
implications for the project schedule, scope, etc.. These changes should not be implemented
until they have been reviewed by the authorized individual(s) and evaluated against all
other project constraints.
- **B Issue a change request to update the procurement management plan**
Incorrect. Apart from the procurement management plan, there are many more components
of the project management plan that may need to be updated. Another answer choice
provides a more comprehensive answer to the question.
- **C Issue a change request to update the project management plan**
Correct. There are many components of the project management plan that may need to be
updated; therefore, a change request should be generated to have them all reviewed and, if
needed, updated.
- **D Deduct the cost of the evaluation process from the vendor's invoice**
Incorrect. There is not enough information in the question to determine if the contract with
the vendor specifies how should the time spent by the project team of the performing
organization evaluating change requests proposed by the vendor be billed. Typically, such
costs are absorbed by the performing organization.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 489-490

Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 107 of 200
Question ID: 613677
- **A project manager who works for a city government is planning a project to build a new**
community center. The project will ultimately be paid for with tax revenues, but the city lacks
the immediate funds that will be required to get the project going. To determine how the project
will be paid, the team is investigating various sources of funding including municipal bonds and
federal grants.
What tool or technique is the team using in this scenario?
Top of Form
- **A Cost aggregation**
- **B Cost baseline**
- **C Financing**
- **D Project funding requirements**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What tool or technique used during the Determine Budget process is helpful in securing funding
for a project?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The scenario implies the project is in the Determine Budget process. One of the tools and
techniques used during this process is financing. Financing entails acquiring funding for projects.

---

It is common for long-term infrastructure, industrial, and public services projects to seek external
sources of funds. The question states that to determine how the project will be paid, the team is
investigating various sources of funding including municipal bonds and federal grants. This
approach is best described by financing, making it the best answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Cost aggregation**
Incorrect. Cost aggregation involves summing the lower-level cost estimates associated
with the various work packages. Cost aggregation is not helpful in obtaining project
funding.
- **B Cost baseline**
Incorrect. The cost baseline is the approved version of the time-phased project budget,
excluding any management reserves. The cost baseline does not deal with the funding
requirements associated with a project.
- **C Financing**
Correct. Financing entails acquiring funding for projects. It is common for long-term
infrastructure, industrial, and public services projects to seek external sources of funds.
- **D Project funding requirements**
Incorrect. Project funding requirements may include the source(s) of funding. However,
project funding requirements is an output of the Determine Budget process, and the
question is asking for a tool or technique.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 253

Question 108 of 200
Question ID: 613841
Your team has been spending an unusual amount of time arguing in meetings. You have
conducted team training to improve meeting discipline and listening skills.
Which document should be updated to reflect the new team standards of conduct?
Top of Form
- **A Issue log**
- **B Team register**
- **C Skill assessments**
- **D Team charter**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Where are team standards recorded?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

This scenario indicates that you are in the Develop Team process. Developing the team's
emotional intelligence and meeting skills are part of this process. The new team standards for
meeting behavior should be recorded as an update to the team charter, which is an output of the
process. This document records team values, agreements, and operating guidelines, as well as
establishes clear expectations for acceptable behavior by the team.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Issue log**
Incorrect. It is reasonable to assume that the issue of arguing in meetings was captured in
the issue log. Therefore, when the issue is resolved, its status should be updated. However,
first, the scenario does not say the issue has already been resolved. Second, the issue log is
not the place to record team standards of conduct.
- **B Team register**
Incorrect. 'Team register' is a made-up term.
- **C Skill assessments**
Incorrect. Skill assessments are considered enterprise environmental factors (EEFs) which
can be updated as an output of the Develop Team process described in the scenario.
However, the team standards of conduct are not captured in this document.
- **D Team charter**
Correct. The team charter records the team's values, agreements, and establishes clear
expectations regarding acceptable team behavior.

**Reference:**

Question 109 of 200
Question ID: 612869
You are the product owner for a retail mobile shopping application developed using an agile
approach. You have envisioned seasonal promotional content and new features based on user
requests. At an upcoming user conference, your customers expect to learn what features have
already been released and what is planned going forward.
What should you present?
Top of Form
- **A The features being developed in the iteration plan**
- **B The user stories included in the iteration plan**
- **C The developer tasks that comprise the user stories**
- **D The product roadmap of features in each iteration**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Think about the level of detail that is appropriate for the intended audience to understand the
schedule of releases.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

This scenario describes agile release planning, which is a tool for the Develop Schedule process.
When presenting a timeline of features to stakeholders at a user conference, the product owner
wants a level of detail that is appropriate for the intended audience. Telling stories is an

---

important presentation skill. However, a 'user story' is an agile term meaning a brief description
of value of the deliverable to a specific user. The product roadmap describes the depth of
information that customers seek, which is an easily understood schedule of features available at
the end of each iteration in each release. The current roadmap would describe features that were
recently released, and what features will be released going forward.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A The features being developed in the iteration plan**
Incorrect. The features being developed in the current iteration may describe what may be
available soon. However, the iteration plan does not help customers understand what
features have been released recently.
- **B The user stories included in the iteration plan**
Incorrect. A user story is a way to describe a feature from the perspective of the user who is
trying to achieve a goal that provides value to them. However, the iteration plan does not
help customers understand what features have been released recently.
- **C The developer tasks that comprise the user stories**
Incorrect. The developer tasks help the development team estimate, plan and manage the
current iteration. However, they are often written in too technical a level to be of interest to
customers at a user conference.
- **D The product roadmap of features in each iteration**
Correct. The roadmap describes exactly the depth of information your customers seek,
which is an easily understood schedule of features available at the end of each iteration in
each release.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 216

Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 110 of 200
Question ID: 651368
- **A supplier the project is using to subcontract some of the project work has delivered all the**
contracted work.
Which value does the project manager attribute to the accepted deliverable?
Top of Form
- **A Net present value**
- **B Earned value**
- **C Accepted value**
- **D Planned value**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What value has been gained from the delivery?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

When project work is being completed and accepted - whether performed by the project team or
component of the project team in the form of a supplier or third party - those results are
considered earned values or EV. The EV is tracked to monitor gains that have been earned over
the course of the project life cycle. The EV can be measured against the planned values (PV) and
the actual costs (AC) of the work to monitor and control the project and to communicate the state

---

of the project. The EV is an example of the data analysis techniques that can be used as part of
the Control Costs process described by the scenario.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Net present value**
Incorrect. Net present value (NPV) is a concept used to determine the value of a project or
undertaking an initiative after factoring all the gains and losses. NPV is not used by
projects to calculate the value earned from the project and components of the project.
- **B Earned value**
Correct. Earned value (EV) is a measure of work performed expressed in terms of the
budget authorized for that work. In the scenario, the work has been accepted and
completed. The deliverable delivers value to the project. As such, the project has earned
value from the result.
- **C Accepted value**
Incorrect. 'Accepted value' is a made-up term.
- **D Planned value**
Incorrect. Planned value (PV) is the authorized budget assigned to schedule work. Based
on the scenario, the deliverable has been accepted. Therefore, the value is no longer
planned but earned.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 261

Question 111 of 200
Question ID: 612715
- **A project manager is conducting the initial process of identifying stakeholders for a new**
infrastructure development project. The project manager has just compiled a list of potential
stakeholders' names.
What should the project manager do next?
Top of Form
- **A Invite the identified stakeholders to the project kick-off meeting**
- **B Conduct stakeholder analysis**
- **C Complete the Project Stakeholder Management process**
- **D Develop the stakeholder engagement plan**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The project is still in the initiation stage and has yet to progress to project planning.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The question suggests that the project is still in the initiation stage, with the initial iteration of the
Identify Stakeholders process, and has yet to progress to project planning. At this point, the
project manager has only compiled a list of potential stakeholders' names. With only a list of
individual and group names, the next logical step is to perform stakeholder analysis. Stakeholder
analysis, an example of the data analysis technique which can be used during the Identify

---

Stakeholder process, results in a list of stakeholders and relevant information such as their
positions in the organization, roles on the project, expectations, attitudes, and their interest in
information about the project. Therefore, of the available choices, conducting stakeholder
analysis is what the project manager should do next.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Invite the identified stakeholders to the project kick-off meeting**
Incorrect. The project kick-off meeting is typically held at the end of project planning and
before the start of project execution. The question suggests that the project is still in the
initiation stage, with the initial pass at the Identify Stakeholders process, and has yet to
progress to project planning. Even if the project manager decided to conduct the kick-off
meeting during the initiation stage, the project manager still needs to perform stakeholder
analysis to determine which of the stakeholders should be invited to the kick-off meeting.
- **B Conduct stakeholder analysis**
Correct. Stakeholder analysis results in a list of stakeholders and relevant information such
as their positions in the organization, roles on the project, expectations, attitudes, and their
interest in information about the project.
- **C Complete the Project Stakeholder Management process**
Incorrect. Project Stakeholder Management is one of the knowledge areas and not a project
management process.
- **D Develop the stakeholder engagement plan**
Incorrect. The question suggests that the project is still in the initiation stage, with the
initial pass at the Identify Stakeholders process, and has yet to progress to project planning.
The stakeholder engagement plan is developed during the Plan Stakeholder Engagement
process as part of project planning. The project manager needs to complete the processes
of the Initiating Process Group before moving on to project planning.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 512

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 7
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 112 of 200
Question ID: 612740
Your enterprise software integration project has just begun execution when your organization
acquires a new subsidiary and involves them in the project. The new subsidiary recently finished
a similar integration project using a compatible tool. Using the tool may accelerate both your
project and the new subsidiary's assimilation into the organization. However, the schedule and
cost variances to take this opportunity do not quite meet agreed-upon risk thresholds.
What should you do?
Top of Form
- **A Do nothing, because the opportunity does not meet your existing stakeholders' risk thresholds as**
documented in your risk management plan.
- **B Ask your project sponsor for permission to switch to the tool that has been used by the new**
subsidiary in their recently completed project.
- **C Submit a change request to adjust the risk thresholds that consider the new stakeholders' risk**
appetite and to update the baselines.
- **D Train your team to use the new tool based on the expert judgment of your new subsidiary's**
integration project team members.
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Consider the appropriate risk strategies for handling specific opportunities, as well as strategies
for overall project risks.
Correct Answer: C

---


**Explanation:**

As you are considering an opportunity to take advantage of a new tool for a project that has just
gotten underway, the scenario indicates you are in the Implement Risk Responses process. You
have five strategies to consider for dealing with specific opportunities: escalate, exploit, share,
enhance, and accept. Considering that your organization has just acquired a new subsidiary, you
should exploit opportunities to capture the benefits of assimilating them into the organization.
Using new technologies to reduce cost and duration are a key example of exploiting an
opportunity.
When it comes to overall project risk, there is a similar set of five strategies to consider: avoid,
exploit, transfer/share, mitigate/enhance, and accept. Where the level of overall project risk is
significantly positive and outside the agreed-upon risk thresholds for the project, an exploit
strategy may be adopted. An example of exploiting at the overall project level would include the
addition of high-benefit elements of scope to the project to add value or benefits to stakeholders.
Alternatively, to embrace the opportunity, the risk thresholds for the project may be modified if
the key stakeholders are in agreement.
Note, the risk thresholds are recorded in the risk management plan to reflect the acceptable level
of overall project risk exposure. Since the risk management plan is a component of the project
management plan, a change request is required to modify any information included in the plan,
such as the risk thresholds.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Do nothing, because the opportunity does not meet your existing stakeholders' risk**
thresholds as documented in your risk management plan.
Incorrect. Doing nothing when there is a clear opportunity from which the project can
benefit (even if the opportunity does not meet the existing risk thresholds) is unlikely to be
the best course of action and is not what a project manager is expected to do.
- **B Ask your project sponsor for permission to switch to the tool that has been used by the**
new subsidiary in their recently completed project.
Incorrect. A change that affects technological resources, staff skills, schedules and costs
would normally require more formality than just asking your sponsor for permission.
- **C Submit a change request to adjust the risk thresholds that consider the new stakeholders'**
risk appetite and to update the baselines.
Correct. The new subsidiary has a new set of stakeholders with different risk appetite. To
embrace the opportunity, the risk thresholds for the project may be modified if the key

---

stakeholders are in agreement. A change request should also address the requisite
adjustments to cost and schedule baselines.
- **D Train your team to use the new tool based on the expert judgment of your new subsidiary's**
integration project team members.
Incorrect. It makes sense to take advantage of the knowledge existing within the integration
team of the new subsidiary to train your team to use the new tool. However, before
spending project resources, you must first resolve the conflict between the opportunity and
the risk thresholds in your risk management plan as well as variances in cost and schedule.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 444-446, 398, 407.
Bottom of Form

Question 113 of 200
Question ID: 613419
Your marketing project started with a team comprised of junior graphics designers. Throughout
the project, you have invested heavily in courses to strengthen the proficiencies of the team
members. Now, you are evaluating the professional knowledge of each team member.
What would be most likely updated as a result of your efforts?
Top of Form
- **A Project team assignments**
- **B Skill assessments**
- **C Individual and team assessments**
- **D Team-building activities**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which of the answer choices is considered an enterprise environmental factor?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The scenario implies that you are involved in the Develop Team process, focusing on the skill
development of your team which is comprised of junior designers. After conducting the intensive
training, you want to validate whether or not the training has achieved its objectives. In other
words, you apply various tools and techniques associated with the Develop Team process to
assess the skills of the team members. The question is asking, "What would be most likely

---

updated as a result of your efforts?" In other words, the question is asking to select an answer
choice that represents one of the outputs of the Develop Team process. Enterprise environmental
factors (EEFs) that can be updated as a result of the Develop Team process include skill
assessments, making this choice the best answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Project team assignments**
Incorrect. Project team assignments is a project document that identifies the team member's
roles and responsibilities. The document will likely be updated when a team member's
project assignment changes, but not when a team member acquires new or improves an
existing skill.
- **B Skill assessments**
Correct. Updates to skill assessments is an example of the enterprise environmental factors
(EEFs) updates which are an output from the Develop Team process implied by the
scenario.
- **C Individual and team assessments**
Incorrect. Individual and team assessments are one of the tools and techniques of the
Develop Team process implied by the scenario. Individual and team assessments are used
by but not updated as a result of this process. The scenario suggests that you have likely
used this tool to evaluate professional knowledge of each individual team member after
providing them with the training to improve their skills.
- **D Team-building activities**
Incorrect. Team building activities are used to build a collaborative and cooperative
working environment. Team building activities are a tool and not an artifact that is updated
as a result of the Develop Team process suggested by the scenario.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page 344

PMP Exam 7

Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 114 of 200
Question ID: 651371
- **A new project manager is brought onto the project. She wants to understand the process by**
which this particular project formally accepts deliverables.
Which of the following will she have to reference?
Top of Form
- **A The scope management plan**
- **B The stakeholder management plan**
- **C The quality management plan**
- **D The requirements management plan**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What provides guidance on how to manage the work of the project?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The scope management plan is a component of the project management plan that contains
information and guidance on how the scope and the scope-related processes are to be managed.
What is included varies, but should contain procedures and processes specifying how the formal
acceptance of the completed project deliverables will be obtained. Acceptance of project
deliverables is influenced by other project management plans, such as the stakeholder

---

management plan and the quality management plan. Nevertheless, the scope management plan is
what specifies the process most directly.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A The scope management plan**
Correct. The scope management plan contains plans and guidance on how the scope
related work is to be managed. This includes the process and procedures for the formal
acceptance of project deliverables.
- **B The stakeholder management plan**
Incorrect. The stakeholder management plan does contain some information about those
accepting the deliverables, but not the process for the acceptance of the deliverables.
- **C The quality management plan**
Incorrect. The quality management plan does contain guidance on the acceptable levels
and specifications of the work but does not lay out the process for the acceptance of
deliverables.
- **D The requirements management plan**
Incorrect. The requirements management plan describes how the project and product
requirements will be analyzed, documented, and managed. This plan does not specify the
process by which the deliverables are accepted.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 137

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 7
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 115 of 200
Question ID: 612876
After activities were estimated and assigned, you created a resource histogram below to show
how many hours each resource was allocated over a series of weeks. Assume they all can do the
same tasks and that it is possible to advance and delay these tasks without violating a scheduling
constraint.
To reduce the risk of burnout and costs of overtime, which of the following choices will address
some of the overallocation displayed?
Top of Form

---

- **A Use available float in the critical path activities to smooth allocation of all team members**
- **B Adjust Etienne's start date so that his tasks for Week 2 begins during Week 1**
- **C Adjust Suri's Week 3 start dates to start in Week 2 and level her utilization for those weeks and**
have her crash some of Kamal's Week 1 tasks
- **D Reassign non-critical staff from another department in the organization**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Looking at the resource histogram shown, consider who is most at risk of overtime costs and
burnout.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The scenario implies you are performing the Develop Schedule process and creating the resource
histogram as one of its outputs. A resource histogram is a model of schedule data that displays
resource requirements and allocations by time period. It often shows the constraint of a 40-hour
work week, which can be used to pinpoint the need for resource optimization in a schedule. The
goal of resource optimization is to reduce the risk of burnout and the costs of overtime. In the
resource histogram, Suri, Kamal, and Robin have the highest weekly over-allocations beyond 40
hours, and Suri also has two weeks of under-allocation. Adjusting the start and finish dates and
sharing workloads (also known as crashing) are two adjustments that can be used for resource
optimization in this scenario. Therefore, of the available choices, adjusting Suri's Week 3 start
dates to start in Week 2 and leveling her utilization for those weeks as well as having her crash
some of Kamal's Week 1 tasks is the best answer to the question asked.
While there are other ways to optimize resources and help Robin who is also over-allocated,
these were not provided as choices. Therefore, one should select the choice that is available and
best addresses the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Use available float in the critical path activities to smooth allocation of all team members**
Incorrect. Resource smoothing does use available float in schedule activities to optimize
resources. However, critical path activities usually have zero float during planning,

---

implying there is no available float on the critical path that can be used to smooth
allocation of the team members.
- **B Adjust Etienne's start date so that his tasks for Week 2 begins during Week 1**
Incorrect. Etienne is least at risk of burnout and overtime. Moving Etienne's four hours
from week 2 to week 1 will leave him idle for week 2 and this will not affect the other
resource allocation issues that are seen in the histogram.
- **C Adjust Suri's Week 3 start dates to start in Week 2 and level her utilization for those weeks**
and have her crash some of Kamal's Week 1 tasks
Correct. Resource leveling is a schedule development technique that involves adjusting
start and finish dates. This technique may also involve adjustments to resource
assignments. As a result, the resource utilization is better balanced with availability.
Accelerating Suri's start dates to level her utilization and having her share Kamal's Week 1
tasks will result in reducing the risk of Kamal experiencing burnout and costs of overtime
beyond a 40-hour work in Week 3, making this choice the best answer to the question
asked.
- **D Reassign non-critical staff from another department in the organization**
Incorrect. Certainly, resource optimization may involve reassigning resources that are not
already assigned critical activities to crash the schedule. However, some of the resources
which are already allocated to this project are readily available. Since some of the
resources on this histogram are under-allocated, they can be reassigned to crash tasks that
are causing others to become over-allocated. This should be done before turning to another
department for help.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 220, 211-212
Bottom of Form

Question 116 of 200
Question ID: 613748
- **A project manager is highly experienced but is new to the organization and industry. He seeks**
assistance from another project manager within the organization that has worked on similar
projects. He meets with that individual in order to get a better understanding of the organization’s
approach to managing risk and the types of risk that are likely to be encountered on the project.
Which one of the tools or techniques is being used in this scenario?
Top of Form
- **A Expert judgment**
- **B Perform Qualitative Risk Analysis**
- **C Perform Quantitative Risk Analysis**
- **D Probability and impact matrix**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Of the available choices, which is a tool or technique associated with the Plan Risk Management
process?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The choices of Perform Qualitative Risk Analysis and Perform Quantitative Risk Analysis can
be eliminated as they are project management processes rather than tools and techniques. The
probability and impact matrix is associated with the Perform Qualitative Risk Analysis process

---

rather than the Plan Risk Management process. Familiarity with the organization’s approach to
managing risk and the types of risk likely to be encountered on the project are examples of
expert judgment.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Expert judgment**
Correct. The new project manager is using expert judgment. The other project manager’s
familiarity with the organization’s approach to managing risk and the types of risk likely to
be encountered on the project are examples of expert judgment.
- **B Perform Qualitative Risk Analysis**
Incorrect. Perform Qualitative Risk Analysis is a project management process and not a
tool or technique.
- **C Perform Quantitative Risk Analysis**
Incorrect. Perform Quantitative Risk Analysis is a project management process and not a
tool or technique.
- **D Probability and impact matrix**
Incorrect. A probability and impact matrix is a grid for mapping the probability of
occurrence of each risk and its impact on project objectives if that risk occurs. The
probability and impact matrix is associated with the Perform Qualitative Risk Analysis
process rather than the Plan Risk Management process and does not contain information
about the organization’s approach to managing risk.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 404

Question 117 of 200
Question ID: 651356
The equipment that is used to connect parts has broken. The maintenance crew has begun repairs
and ordered replacement parts per the response plan. The crew expects the equipment to be down
for at least three days.
What should the project manager do next?
Top of Form
- **A Submit a change request to update the procurement management plan**
- **B Inform all affected stakeholders of the situation and the response plan**
- **C Order extra parts to store in the warehouse in case the machine breaks again**
- **D Document the knowledge gained in the lessons learned register**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Communication is an important duty of any project manager.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

As known project risks are realized, the risk response plans are implemented as part of the
Implement Risk Responses process. Risk report is a project document developed progressively
throughout the Project Risk Management processes, which summarizes information on
individual project risks and the level of overall project risk. Updates to the risk report are among
the outputs of the Implement Risk Responses process. The project manager must communicate

---

what is happening and the impacts of the project to stakeholders. Sharing the risk report with the
stakeholders is an example of communications that can be done as part of the process described
in the scenario. It is the project manager's responsibility to ensure information is sent out
appropriately and understood by the recipients. Hence, of the choices provided, informing all
affected stakeholders of the situation and the response plan is the best answer to the question
asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Submit a change request to update the procurement management plan**
Incorrect. The procurement management plan describes how the project will acquire goods
and services from outside of the performing organization. There is nothing in the scenario
that indicates the way goods and services are acquired should be changed as a result of the
crew ordering replacement parts.
- **B Inform all affected stakeholders of the situation and the response plan**
Correct. Communication regarding a realized risk and its response is of importance to all
affected stakeholders. This is the best action of the project manager at this point.
- **C Order extra parts to store in the warehouse in case the machine breaks again**
Incorrect. The crew is responding to the realized risk per the risk response plans. There is
no information mentioned in the plan instructing the project manager to procure and store
additional equipment. Doing so may be physically impractical or budget constrained.
- **D Document the knowledge gained in the lessons learned register**
Incorrect. While it is beneficial that the lessons learned register is updated with risk
response strategies that worked well, there is nothing in the question to indicate that any
specific knowledge has been gained. All the project team has done was ordering
replacement parts.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 452

Question 118 of 200
Question ID: 613405
You are in the process of obtaining the necessary equipment for your construction project. A
review of the resource calendar indicates that there is a scheduling conflict with the excavator
needed for the site preparation. You have decided to resolve the conflict by substituting the
excavator with a larger model which is currently available.
What should you do next?
Top of Form
- **A Update the project schedule**
- **B Modify the project charter**
- **C Revise the resource requirements**
- **D Submit a change request to adjust the cost baseline**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Where should you document the types and quantities of resources required for each activity in a
work package?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The question implies that the project manager is performing the Acquire Resources process by
obtaining an excavator to be used for the site preparation. The resource requirements is one of
the project documents that may be updated during this process. The resource requirements

---

document the types and quantities of resources required for each activity in a work package.
Since the excavator was substituted with a larger model, the resource requirements need to be
updated to reflect the resource actually acquired for use on the project. Therefore, of the
available choices, revising the resource requirements is what you should do next.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Update the project schedule**
Incorrect. The project schedule will not likely be affected by substituting a required
resource for a different one that is capable of performing the same work during the
required timeframe.
- **B Modify the project charter**
Incorrect. The project charter only contains high-level information about the project. It is
not likely to include details such as the type of excavator that will be used on the project.
- **C Revise the resource requirements**
Correct. The resource requirements document the types and quantities of resources required
for each activity in a work package. Since the excavator was substituted with a larger
model, the resource requirements need to be updated to reflect the resources acquired for
the project.
- **D Submit a change request to adjust the cost baseline**
Incorrect. The question does not state whether or not the larger excavator will cost more
(or less) than the model originally planned.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 335

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 7
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 119 of 200
Question ID: 612304
The project you are managing is well underway, and you are currently actively collecting and
storing information about the progress of project deliverables, creating forecasts for your
sponsor, distributing work performance reports, and presenting project status to key stakeholders.
Which process are you performing?
Top of Form
- **A Manage Communications**
- **B Manage Stakeholder Engagement**
- **C Monitor Communications**
- **D Plan Communications Management**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

First, consider which knowledge area the activities described are principally concerned. Then,
determine which process group and process these activities would take place.
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

To answer this question, first, determine under which knowledge area the described activities
fall. With reference to sponsors and stakeholders, you may guess that it is Stakeholder
Management. However, the activities of collection, creation, distribution, storage, and
monitoring project information fall under Communications Management.

---

Next, determine what process group is related to these activities. Is it the Planning Process Group
or Monitoring and Controlling Process Group? No, the task is not to develop the communication
models (which would have been part of project planning) in planning, nor is the task to
determine if the planned communications artifacts and activities have had the desired effect
(which would have been part of monitoring and controlling). Instead, the current activities are
mostly collection, creation, distribution, and disposition of project information, which take place
while the work of the project is being executed. In other words, you are in the Executing Process
Group, under the Project Communications Management Knowledge Area, i.e., you are carrying
out the Manage Communications process.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Manage Communications**
Correct. Manage Communications is the process of ensuring timely and appropriate
collection, creation, distribution, storage, retrieval, management, monitoring, and the
ultimate disposition of project information.
- **B Manage Stakeholder Engagement**
Incorrect. Manage Stakeholder Engagement is the process of communicating and working
with stakeholders to meet their needs and expectations, address issues, and foster
appropriate stakeholder involvement. This process is focused on stakeholders while in the
scenario, you are more concerned with the information itself rather than working with
stakeholders to meet their needs and expectations.
- **C Monitor Communications**
Incorrect. Monitor Communications is the process of ensuring that the planned
communications artifacts and activities effectively meet the needs of the project and its
stakeholders. In the scenario, you are collecting and storing information about the progress
of project deliverables, creating forecasts for your sponsor, distributing work performance
reports, and presenting project status to key stakeholders. Those activities do not fall under
the Monitor Communications process.
- **D Plan Communications Management**
Incorrect. Plan Communications Management is the process of developing an appropriate
approach, models, and plans for project communication activities based on the information
needs of each stakeholder or group, available organizational assets, and the needs of the
project. The scenario implies the project is in execution rather than planning.

**Reference:**


---

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 379, 387

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 7
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 120 of 200
Question ID: 651380
The project is not getting the marketing team to update the content of the online magazine
website as scheduled. The outdated content is causing confusion among readers.
What can the project manager do to engage the marketing team and make the needed changes as
soon as possible?
Top of Form
- **A Force the marketing manager to make the changes immediately**
- **B Communicate the importance and urgency of the change**
- **C Assign any another project team member to perform the work**
- **D Complain to other managers about the lack of response time**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What is within the sphere of influence and power of the project manager?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

Managing stakeholder engagement throughout a project is a difficult, yet important, process.
Communicating and working with project stakeholders to meet project and stakeholder needs
and expectations require interpersonal skills and leveraging other tools and techniques. In this
scenario, for unknown reasons, the stakeholders in the marketing team are not available for the
project as scheduled. Of the choices available, communicating the urgency and importance of the

---

project to the stakeholders falls within the authority of the project manager and is likely to be the
best course of action for the project manager to take under current circumstances. Forcing or
threatening or making others perform the work without proper communication with the
stakeholders risks breakdown of trust, cooperation, and shared values.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Force the marketing manager to make the changes immediately**
Incorrect. A project manager's sphere of influence is not one who can control or force
action of a functional manager within an organization. Better interpersonal approaches are
advised. Note, since the scenario mentions marketing team, it can be implied the
organizational structure is not projectized and, therefore, the project manager does not
have the full authority over resources.
- **B Communicate the importance and urgency of the change**
Correct. The marketing team stakeholders are not engaged because they are probably not
aware of the urgency and importance of the request. Communicating the need and priority
can negotiate a better timing on the schedule.
- **C Assign any another project team member to perform the work**
Incorrect. The marketing team is assigned the work. Reassigning the activities to any other
project team member discredits the skill set and other related work needs, abilities, and
procedures of the marketing team, as well as does not guarantee success since it is unclear
if another team member possesses the skills needed to complete the task.
- **D Complain to other managers about the lack of response time**
Incorrect. Communicating non-productive complaints that do not assist in the work getting
done is no help. Discussing displeasure with others not immediately involved in the concern
brings in irrelevant actors and causes unnecessary disruption and gossip.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 523-524

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 7
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 121 of 200
Question ID: 613234
- **A project manager is currently in the process of prioritizing individual project risks by assessing**
their detectability, proximity, and impact value. The project manager would like to create a
graphical representation of these three dimensions.
What is the best course of action?
Top of Form
- **A Generate a RACI chart**
- **B Prepare a requirements traceability matrix**
- **C Develop a bubble chart**
- **D Create a probability and impact matrix**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What type of graphical representation can display three rather than just two parameters?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

Perform Qualitative Risk Analysis is the process of prioritizing individual project risks for
further analysis or action by assessing their probability of occurrence and impact as well as other
characteristics such as detectability, proximity, and impact value. Thus, the project manager is
conducting the Perform Qualitative Risk Analysis process and needs to create a graphical
representation of project risks along three dimensions. A data representation technique that may

---

be used in support of this process includes hierarchical charts, of which bubble charts are an
example. A bubble chart displays three dimensions of data, where each risk is plotted as a disk
(bubble), and the three parameters are presented by the X-axis value, the Y-axis value, and the
bubble size. In this scenario, the detectability and proximity can be plotted on the X and Y axes,
and the impact value represented by the bubble size. The incorrect answer choices describe
charts that can only display two parameters rather than three.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Generate a RACI chart**
Incorrect. A RACI chart is a common type of responsibility assignment matrix that uses
responsible, accountable, consult, and inform statuses to define the involvement of
stakeholders in project activities. However, the question is asking about a graphical
representation of project risks rather than aspects of stakeholder involvement.
- **B Prepare a requirements traceability matrix**
Incorrect. A requirements traceability matrix is a grid that links product requirements from
their origin to the deliverables that satisfy them. The requirements traceability matrix is not
used as a graphical representation of project risks.
- **C Develop a bubble chart**
Correct. A bubble chart displays three dimensions of data, where each risk is plotted as a
disk (bubble), and the three parameters are presented by the X-axis value, the Y-axis value,
and the bubble size. In this scenario, the detectability and proximity can be plotted on the X
and Y axes, and the impact value can be represented by the bubble size.
- **D Create a probability and impact matrix**
Incorrect. A probability and impact matrix is a grid for mapping the probability of
occurrence of each risk and its impact on project objectives if that risk occurs. Although a
probability and impact matrix is a data representation technique that may be used in the
Perform Qualitative Risk Analysis process, the probability and impact matrix can only
display two and not three parameters.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 425-426
Bottom of Form

Question 122 of 200
Question ID: 613750
As a project manager, you will need the assistance of other stakeholders in order to identify the
risks associated with your project. You want to determine who are the individuals that might
participate in the process of identifying risks to the project, as well as those who are available to
act as risk owners.
Where should you look?
Top of Form
- **A Responsibility assignment matrix (RAM)**
- **B Project charter**
- **C Risk breakdown structure (RBS)**
- **D Stakeholder register**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What input to the Identify Risks process contains the identification, assessment, and
classification of project stakeholders?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The question implies that the project team is performing the project management process of
Identify Risks. One input to this process is the stakeholder register. The stakeholder register is a
project document that lists project stakeholders along with their identification and assessment

---

information, and classification. The project manager can use this information to find out which
individuals or groups might participate in identifying risks to the project as well as to determine
those stakeholders who are available to act as risk owners. The stakeholder register is the best
place to find which stakeholders should be included in the Identify Risks process.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Responsibility assignment matrix (RAM)**
Incorrect. The responsibility assignment matrix (RAM) is a grid that shows the project
resources assigned to each work package. The RAM is used to illustrate the connections
between work packages and project team members and would be less helpful in identifying
stakeholders that might participate in risk identification or act as risk owners.
- **B Project charter**
Incorrect. The project charter is issued by the sponsor and authorizes the existence of a
project. It may contain high-level information on risks but does not have information on
which stakeholders might participate in identifying risks to the project.
- **C Risk breakdown structure (RBS)**
Incorrect. The risk breakdown structure is a hierarchical representation of potential
sources of risks. It does not contain information on which stakeholders might participate in
identifying risks to the project.
- **D Stakeholder register**
Correct. Information included in the stakeholder register can help the project manager to
understand which individuals or groups might participate in identifying risks to the project
as well as those who are available to act as risk owners.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 413

Question ID: 613747
To complete the Plan Risk Management process and establish risk thresholds for your project,
you want to get a better understanding of the key stakeholder’s attitudes toward risk.
Where is the best place to find this information?

What input to the Plan Risk Management process contains information on key stakeholder’s

process is the stakeholder register. The stakeholder register contains details of the project’s
stakeholders and provides an overview of their project roles and their attitude toward risk on the
project. This information is useful in setting risk thresholds for the project.

---

- **B Risk management plan**
